Question #1 (ID: 805257)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{x}^{4}+\mathrm{x}^{2} \mathrm{y}^{2}+\mathrm{y}^{4}=27, \mathrm{x}^{2}+\mathrm{xy}+\mathrm{y}^{2}=9 \\\text { এবং } l=3^{\mathrm{m}}+3^{1-\mathrm{m}} .[/math]রা. বো.'2024

Options:
ক. <p>\( p^{4}+p^{2}-2 \) কে উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর।</p>

খ. <p>প্রমাণ কর যে, \( 3 \mathrm{xy}\left(\mathrm{x}^{2}+\mathrm{y}^{2}\right)=54 \).</p>

গ. <p>\( l=4 \) হলে, m এর মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>



Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক[math]\begin{aligned} \mathrm{p}^4+\mathrm{p}^2-2 &amp; =\mathrm{p}^4-1+\mathrm{p}^2-1 \\ &amp; =\left(\mathrm{p}^2\right)^2-1^2+\mathrm{p}^2-1 \\ &amp; =\left(\mathrm{p}^2-1\right)\left(\mathrm{p}^2+1\right)+\left(\mathrm{p}^2-1\right)\end{aligned}[/math][math]\begin{aligned} &amp; =\left(p^2-1\right)\left(p^2+1+1\right) \\ &amp; =\left(p^2-1^2\right)\left(p^2+2\right)=(p+1)(p-1)\left(p^2+2\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, \( x^{4}+x^{2} y^{2}+y^{4}=27&hellip;&hellip;..(i) \)এবং \( x^{2}+x y+y^{2}=9 &hellip;&hellip;&hellip;.(ii)\)(i) নং হতে পাই, \( x^{4}+x^{2} y^{2}+y^{4}=27 \)বা, \( \left(x^{2}\right)^{2}+2 \cdot x^{2} \cdot y^{2}+\left(y^{2}\right)^{2}-x^{2} y^{2}=27 \)বা, \( \left(x^{2}+y^{2}\right)^{2}-(x y)^{2}=27 \)বা, \( \left(\mathrm{x}^{2}+\mathrm{y}^{2}+\mathrm{xy}\right)\left(\mathrm{x}^{2}+\mathrm{y}^{2}-\mathrm{xy}\right)=27 \)বা, \( 9\left(x^{2}-x y+y^{2}\right)=27 \)বা, \( x^{2}-x y+y^{2}=3&hellip;&hellip;&hellip;.(iii) \)এখন, (ii) ও (iii) নং যোগ করে পাই, \( 2 x^{2}+2 y^{2}=9+3=12 \)বা, \( x^{2}+y^{2}=\frac{12}{2}=6 &hellip;&hellip;..(iv)\)\( \mathrm{x}^{2}+\mathrm{y}^{2} \) এর মান (ii) নং এ বসিয়ে পাই, \( 6+\mathrm{xy}=9 \)\( \begin{array}{l} \text { বা, } x y=9-6=3 \text {....................(v) } \\ \text { বামপক্ষ }=3 x y\left(x^{2}+y^{2}\right) \\ =3.3 .6 \text { [(iv) ও (v) নং হতে] } \end{array} \)\(​​​​​​​= 54 =\) ডানপক্ষ\( \begin{array}{l} \therefore 3 x y\left(x^{2}+y^{2}\right)=54 \text {.(প্রমাণিত) } \end{array} \)
গদেওয়া আছে, \( l=3^{\mathrm{m}}+3^{1-\mathrm{m}} \)এখন, \( l=4 \) হলে, \( 3^{\mathrm{m}}+3^{1-\mathrm{m}}=4 \)বা, \( 3^{\mathrm{m}}+\frac{3}{3^{\mathrm{m}}}=4 \)বা, \( a+\frac{3}{a}=4\left[3^{m}=a\right. \) ধরে \( ] \)বা, \( a^{2}+3=4 a \)বা, \( a^{2}-4 a+3=0 \)বা, \( a^{2}-3 a-a+3=0 \)বা, \( a(a-3)-1(a-3)=0 \)বা, \( (a-3)(a-1)=0 \)হয়, \( a-3=0 \)বা, \( a=3 \)বা, \( 3^{m}=3^{1} \)\( \therefore \quad \mathrm{m}=1 \)অথবা, \( a-1=0 \)বা, \( a=1 \)বা, \( 3^{\mathrm{m}}=3^{0} \)\( \therefore \mathrm{m}=0 \)নির্ণেয় মান \( \mathrm{m}=1,0 \).
ঘ

Question #2 (ID: 805258)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\begin{array}{l} \mathrm{A}=\{\mathrm{x}: \mathrm{x} \text { মৌলিক সংখ্যা এবং } \mathrm{x}&lt;4\} \\ \mathrm{M}=\{\mathrm{x} \in \mathbb{Z}:-3&lt;\mathrm{x}&lt;3\} \\ \mathrm{N}=\{\mathrm{x} \in \mathbb{N}: \mathrm{x} \leq 3\} \text { এবং } \mathrm{y}^{6}-42 \sqrt{6} \mathrm{y}^{3}+1=0 \end{array}[/math]চ. বো.'2024

Options:
ক. <p>\( \mathrm{A} \times \mathrm{A} \) নির্ণয় কর।</p>

খ. <p>\( \mathrm{C}=\mathrm{M} \backslash \mathrm{N} \) হলে দেখাও যে, C এর উপাদান সংখ্যা n হলে \( \mathrm{P}(\mathrm{C}) \) এর উপাদান সংখ্যা \( 2^{\mathrm{n}} \) সমর্থন করে।</p>

গ. <p>দেখাও যে, \( y=\sqrt{6}+\sqrt{5} \).</p>



Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{A}=\{\mathrm{x}: \mathrm{x} \) মৌলিক সংখ্যা এবং \( \mathrm{x}&lt;4\} \)অর্থাৎ, যেসব মৌলিক সংখ্যা 4 অপেক্ষা ছোট তাদের সেট A।4 অপেক্ষা ছোট মৌলিক সংখ্যাগুলো হলো : 2, 3\( \begin{array}{l} \therefore \quad A=\{2,3\} \\ \therefore \quad A \times A=\{2,3\} \times\{2,3\}\\=\{(2,2),(2,3),(3,2),(3,3)\} \end{array} \)নির্ণেয় \( A \times A=\{(2,2),(2,3),(3,2),(3,3)\} \).
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]M=\{x \in \mathbb{Z}:-3&lt;x&lt;3\}[/math]অর্থাৎ, যেসব পূর্ণসংখ্যা - 3 অপেক্ষা বড় এবং 3 অপেক্ষা ছোট তাদের সেট M।এখন, -3 অপেক্ষা বড় এবং 3 অপেক্ষা ছোট পূর্ণসংখ্যাসমূহ হলো :\( \begin{array}{l} -2,-1,0,1,2 \\ \therefore \quad M=\{-2,-1,0,1,2\} \\ N=\{x \in \mathbb{N}: x \leq 3\} \end{array} \)অর্থাৎ, যেসব স্বাভাবিক সংখ্যা 3 এর ছোট অথবা 3 এর সমান তাদের সেট N।এখন, 3 এর ছোট অথবা 3 এর সমান স্বাভাবিক সংখ্যাসমূহ হলো:\( 1,2,3 \).এখন, C = M\N হলে,[math]C=\{-2,-1,0,1,2\} \backslash\{1,2,3\}=\{-2,-1,0\}[/math][math]\therefore \quad P(C)=\{\phi,\{-2\},\{-1\},\{0\}[/math],[math]\{-2,-1\},\{-2,0\}[/math],[math]\{-1,0\},\{-2,-1,0\}\}[/math]এখানে, C সেটের উপাদান সংখ্যা, \( \mathrm{n}=3 \)\( P(C) \) সেটের উপাদান সংখ্যা \( =8=2^{3}=2^{n} \)\( \therefore \mathrm{P}(\mathrm{C}) \) এর উপাদান সংখ্যা \( 2^{\mathrm{n}} \) কে সমর্থন করে। (দেখানো হলো)
গদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{y}^{6}-42 \sqrt{6} \mathrm{y}^{3}+1=0 \)বা, \( \left(y^{3}\right)^{2}-2 . y^{3} \cdot 21 \\\sqrt{6}+(21 \sqrt{6})^{2}-(21 \sqrt{6})^{2}+1=0 \)বা, \( \left(y^{3}-21 \sqrt{6}\right)^{2}-2646+1=0 \)বা, \( \left(y^{3}-21 \sqrt{6}\right)^{2}-2645=0 \)বা, \( \left(y^{3}-21 \sqrt{6}\right)^{2}=2645 \)বা, \( y^{3}-21 \sqrt{6}=\sqrt{2645} \) [বর্গমূল করে]বা, \( y^{3}-21 \sqrt{6}=23 \sqrt{5} \)বা, \( y^{3}=21 \sqrt{6}+23 \sqrt{5} \)বা, \( y^{3}=6 \sqrt{6}+18 \sqrt{5}+15 \sqrt{6}+5 \sqrt{5} \)বা, \( y^{3}=(\sqrt{6})^{3}+3 \cdot(\sqrt{6})^{2} \cdot \sqrt{5}\\+3 \sqrt{6} \cdot(\sqrt{5})^{2}+(\sqrt{5})^{3} \)বা, \( y^{3}=(\sqrt{6}+\sqrt{5})^{3} \)\( \therefore \quad y=\sqrt{6}+\sqrt{5} \). (দেখানো হলো)
ঘ

Question #3 (ID: 805259)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{p}^{2}-9=4 \sqrt{5}[/math]সি. বো.'2024

Options:
ক. <p>প্রমাণ কর যে, \( p=\sqrt{5}+2 \).</p>

খ. <p>\( \mathrm{p}^{4}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{4}} \) এর মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>

গ. <p>প্রমাণ কর যে, \( \mathrm{p}^{5}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{3}}=610 \sqrt{5} \).</p>



Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{p}^{2}-9=4 \sqrt{5} \)বা, \( \mathrm{p}^{2}=9+4 \sqrt{5} \)বা, \( \mathrm{p}^{2}=5+4 \sqrt{5}+4 \)বা, \( \mathrm{p}^{2}=(\sqrt{5})^{2}+2 \sqrt{5} \cdot 2+2^{2} \)বা, \( p^{2}=(\sqrt{5}+2)^{2} \)বা, \( p=\sqrt{5}+2 \) [বর্গমূল করে]\( \therefore \quad p=\sqrt{5}+2 \). (প্রমাণিত)
খদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{p}^{2}-9=4 \sqrt{5} \)বা, \( \mathrm{p}^{2}=9+4 \sqrt{5} \)বা, \( \frac{1}{p^{2}}=\frac{1}{9+4 \sqrt{5}} \)বা, \( \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{2}}=\frac{1(9-4 \sqrt{5})}{(9+4 \sqrt{5})(9-4 \sqrt{5})}=\frac{9-4 \sqrt{5}}{9^{2}-(4 \sqrt{5})^{2}}=\frac{9-4 \sqrt{5}}{81-80} \)\( \therefore \quad \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{2}}=9-4 \sqrt{5} \)এখন, \( \mathrm{p}^{2}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{2}}=9+4 \sqrt{5}+9-4 \sqrt{5}=18 \)&hellip;&hellip;..(i)\( \mathrm{p}^{2}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{2}}=9+4 \sqrt{5}-9+4 \sqrt{5}=8 \sqrt{5} \)&hellip;&hellip;&hellip;&hellip;(ii)প্রদত্ত রাশি \( =p^{4}-\frac{1}{p^{4}} \)\( \begin{array}{l} =\left(\mathrm{p}^{2}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{2}}\right)^{2} \\ =\left(\mathrm{p}^{2}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{2}}\right)\left(\mathrm{p}^{2}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{2}}\right) \\ =18 \cdot 8 \sqrt{5}[(\mathrm{i}) \text { ও (ii) নং হতে পাই] } \\ =144 \sqrt{5} \end{array} \)নির্ণেয় মান : \( 144 \sqrt{5} \).
গ'ক' হতে পাই, \( \mathrm{p}=\sqrt{5}+2 \)[math]\therefore \quad \frac{1}{p}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{5}+2}[math]=\frac{\sqrt{5}-2}{(\sqrt{5}+2)(\sqrt{5}-2)}=\frac{\sqrt{5}-2}{(\sqrt{5})^2-2^2}=\frac{\sqrt{5}-2}{5-4}=\sqrt{5}-2[/math]\therefore \quad[/math] p. [math]+\frac{1}{p}=\sqrt{5}+2+\sqrt{5}-2=2 \sqrt{5}[math]p^2+\frac{1}{p^2}=\left(p+\frac{1}{p}\right)^2-2 \cdot p \cdot \frac{1}{p}\\=(2 \sqrt{5})^2-2=20-2=18[/math][math]\mathrm{p}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^3}=\left(\mathrm{p}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}\right)^3-3 \cdot \mathrm{p} \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}\left(\mathrm{p}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}\right)[/math]=(2 \sqrt{5})^3-3 \times 2 \sqrt{5}=40 \sqrt{5}-6 \sqrt{5}=34 \sqrt{5}[/math]\( \begin{array}{l} \text { বামপক্ষ }=p^{5}+\frac{1}{p^{3}} \\ =\left(\mathrm{p}^{3}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{3}}\right)\left(\mathrm{p}^{2}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{2}}\right)-\left(\mathrm{p}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}\right) \\ =34 \sqrt{5} \times 18-2 \sqrt{5} \text { [মান বসিয়ে] } \\ =612 \sqrt{5}-2 \sqrt{5}=610 \sqrt{5}=\text { ডানপক্ষ} \\ \therefore \mathrm{p}^{5}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{5}}=610 \sqrt{5} \text {. (প্রমাণিত) } \end{array} \)
ঘ

Question #4 (ID: 805260)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x=\frac{\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2}}{3}, y=\sqrt{5}-\sqrt{2}[/math]চ. বো.'2023

Options:
ক. <p>\( (2 a-b)^{3}-27 \) কে উৎপাদকে বিশ্নেষণ কর।</p>

খ. <p>\( 3 x y\left(9 x^{2}+y^{2}\right) \) এর মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>

গ. <p>প্রমাণ কর যে, \( \frac{27}{y^{3}}-y^{3}=34 \sqrt{2} \).</p>



Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \text {}(2 a-b)^3-27 \\ &amp; =(2 a-b)^3-(3)^3\end{aligned}[math]=(2 \mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b}-3)\left\{(2 \mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})^2+(2 \mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b}) \cdot 3+3^2\right\}[/math]\begin{aligned} &amp; =(2 a-b-3)\left(4 a^2-4 a b+b^2+6 a-3 b+9\right) \\ &amp; =(2 a-b-3)\left(4 a^2+b^2-4 a b+6 a-3 b+9\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, \( x=\frac{\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2}}{3} \)বা, \( 3 x=\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2} \)এবং \( \mathrm{y}=\sqrt{5}-\sqrt{2} \)\( \therefore \quad 3 x+y=\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2}+\sqrt{5}-\sqrt{2}=2 \sqrt{5} \)এবং \( 3 x-y=\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2}-\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2}=2 \sqrt{2} \)প্রদত্ত রাশি \( =3 x y\left(9 x^{2}+y^{2}\right) \)[math]=\frac{1}{8} \cdot 4 \cdot 3 x \cdot y \cdot 2\left(9 x^2+y^2\right)[math]=\frac{1}{8}\left\{(3 x+y)^2-(3 x-y)^2\right\}\\\left\{(3 x+y)^2+(3 x-y)^2\right\}[/math]=\frac{1}{8}\left\{(2 \sqrt{5})^2-(2 \sqrt{2})^2\right\}\left\{(2 \sqrt{5})^2+(2 \sqrt{2})^2\right\}[/math][math]=\frac{1}{8}(20-8)(20+8)=\frac{1}{8} \times 12 \times 28 = 42[/math]নির্ণেয় মান : 42.
গদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{y}=\sqrt{5}-\sqrt{2} \)\( \therefore \quad \frac{1}{y}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{5}-\sqrt{2}} \)বা, \( \frac{3}{y}=\frac{3}{\sqrt{5}-\sqrt{2}} \)\( \begin{array}{l} =\frac{3(\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2})}{(\sqrt{5}-\sqrt{2})(\sqrt{5}+2)} \\ =\frac{3(\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2})}{(\sqrt{5})^{2}-(\sqrt{2})^{2}} \\ =\frac{3(\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2})}{5-2}=\frac{3(\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2})}{3}=\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2} \\ \therefore \quad \frac{3}{y}-y=\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2}-\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{2}=2 \sqrt{2} \text {. } \\ \text { বামপক্ষ }=\frac{27}{y^{3}}-y^{3} \\ =\left(\frac{3}{y}\right)^{3}-y^{3} \\ =\left(\frac{3}{y}-y\right)^{3}+3 \cdot \frac{3}{y} \cdot y\left(\frac{3}{y}-y\right) \\ =(2 \sqrt{2})^{3}+9 \times 2 \sqrt{2} \\ =16 \sqrt{2}+18 \sqrt{2}=34 \sqrt{2}=\text { ডানপক্ষ} \\ \therefore \frac{27}{\mathrm{y}^{3}}-\mathrm{y}^{3}=34 \sqrt{2} \text {. (প্রমাণিত) } \end{array} \)
ঘ

Question #5 (ID: 805261)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]y=\sqrt{5}-2 \text { এবং } x+y=2 \sqrt{5}[/math]দি. বো.'2023

Options:
ক. <p>উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর : \( 2-5 x-12 x^{2} \).</p>

খ. <p>\( \frac{1}{y^{3}}-y^{3} \) এর মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>

গ. <p>প্রমাণ কর যে, \( \mathrm{xy}\left(\mathrm{x}^{2}+\mathrm{y}^{2}\right)=18 \).</p>



Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক[math]\begin{aligned} \text { প্রদত্ত রাশি } &amp; =2-5 x-12 x^2 \\ &amp; =2+3 x-8 x-12 x^2\end{aligned}[/math][math]=1(2+3 x)-4 x(2+3 x)=(2+3 x)(1-4 x)[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{y}=\sqrt{5}-2[math]\therefore \quad \frac{1}{y}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{5}-2}=\frac{\sqrt{5}+2}{(\sqrt{5}+2)(\sqrt{5}-2)}[/math]=\frac{\sqrt{5}+2}{(\sqrt{5})^2-2^2}=\frac{\sqrt{5}+2}{5-4}=\sqrt{5}+2[math]\therefore \quad \frac{1}{y}-y=\sqrt{5}+2-\sqrt{5}+2=4[/math]প্রদত্ত রাশি =[math]=\frac{1}{y^3}-y^3=\left(\frac{1}{y}-y\right)^3+3 \cdot \frac{1}{y} \cdot y\left(\frac{1}{y}-y\right)[/math]=4^3+3 \times 4=64+12=76[/math]নির্ণেয় মান: 76.
গদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{y}=\sqrt{5}-2 \)এবং \( \mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y}=2 \sqrt{5} \).বা, \( x+\sqrt{5}-2=2 \sqrt{5} \quad[\because y=\sqrt{5}-2] \)বা, \( x=2 \sqrt{5}-\sqrt{5}+2 \)\( \begin{array}{ll} \therefore &amp; x=\sqrt{5}+2 \\ \therefore &amp; x-y=\sqrt{5}+2-\sqrt{5}+2=4 \end{array} \)বামপক্ষ \( =x y\left(x^{2}+y^{2}\right) \)[math]=\frac{1}{8} \cdot 4 x y \cdot 2\left(x^2+y^2\right)[math]=\frac{1}{8}\left\{(x+y)^2-(x-y)^2\right\}\left\{(x+y)^2+(x-y)^2\right\}[/math]=\frac{1}{8}\left\{(2 \sqrt{5})^2-4^2\right\}\left\{(2 \sqrt{5})^2+4^2\right\}[/math][math]=\frac{1}{8}(20-16)(20+16)=\frac{1}{8} \times 4 \times 36=18=[/math]ডানপক্ষ\( \therefore \mathrm{xy}\left(\mathrm{x}^{2}+\mathrm{y}^{2}\right)=18 \). (প্রমাণিত)
ঘ

Question #6 (ID: 805262)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=x^{4}+\frac{1}{x^{4}}, B=y^{4}-y^{2}+1[/math]ভিকারুননিসা নূন স্কুল এন্ড কলেজ, ঢাকা'

Options:
ক. <p>যদি \( (x+y, 6)=(0, x-y) \) হয়, তাহলে \( (x, y) \) এর মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>

খ. <p>যদি \( \mathrm{A}=119 \) হয়, তাহলে দেখাও যে, \( \mathrm{x}=3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}} \)</p>

গ. <p>যদি \( \mathrm{B}=0 \) হয়, তাহলে প্রমাণ কর যে, \( \left(\frac{y^{6}+1}{y^{3}}\right)\left(y^{2}-\frac{1}{y^{2}}\right)=0 \).</p>



Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, \( (x+y, 6)=(0, x-y) \)ক্রমজোড়ের শর্তানুসারে,\( \begin{array}{l} x+y=0&hellip;&hellip;&hellip;.(i) \\ x-y=6&hellip;&hellip;&hellip;.(ii) \end{array} \)(1) নং ও (2) নং সমীকরণ যোগ করে পাই,\( x+y+x-y=0+6 \)বা, \( 2 x=6 \)বা, \( x=\frac{6}{2} \)\( \therefore \quad x=3 \)\( \therefore \quad \) (1) নং সমীকরণে x এর মান বসিয়ে পাই,\( 3+y=0 \)\( \therefore \quad y=-3 \)নির্ণেয় মান : \( (x, y)=(3,-3) \)
খদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{A}=\mathrm{x}^{4}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^{4}} \)এখন, \( A=119 \) হলে,\( x^{4}+\frac{1}{x^{4}}=119 \)বা, \( \left(x^{2}\right)^{2}+\left(\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)^{2}=119 \)বা, \( \left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot x^{2} \cdot \frac{1}{x^{2}}=119 \)বা, \( \left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)^{2}-2=119 \)বা, \( \left(\mathrm{x}^{2}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^{2}}\right)^{2}=119+2 \)বা, \( \left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)^{2}=121 \)বা, \( \mathrm{x}^{2}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^{2}}=\sqrt{121} \) [বর্গমূল করে]বা, \( x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}=11 \)বা, \( \left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}+2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=11 \)বা, \( \left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}+2=11 \)বা, \( \left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=11-2 \)বা, \( \left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}=9 \)বা, \( x-\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{9} \) [বর্গমূল করে]বা, \( x-\frac{1}{x}=3 \)\( \therefore \quad x=3+\frac{1}{x} \) (দেখানো হলো)
গদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{B}=\mathrm{y}^{4}-\mathrm{y}^{2}+1 \)এখন, \( \mathrm{B}=0 \) হলে, \( \mathrm{y}^{4}-\mathrm{y}^{2}+1=0 \)বা, \( y^{4}+1=y^{2} \)বা, \( \frac{\mathrm{y}^{4}+1}{\mathrm{y}^{2}}=\frac{\mathrm{y}^{2}}{\mathrm{y}^{2}} \)বা, \( y^{2}+\frac{1}{y^{2}}=1 \)বা, \( \left(y+\frac{1}{y}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot y \cdot \frac{1}{y}=1 \)বা, \( \left(y+\frac{1}{y}\right)^{2}-2=1 \)বা, \( \left(y+\frac{1}{y}\right)^{2}=1+2 \)বা, \( \left(y+\frac{1}{y}\right)^{2}=3 \)\( \therefore \quad y+\frac{1}{y}=\sqrt{3} \) [বর্গমূল করে]\( \begin{array}{l} \text { এখন, } \frac{\mathrm{y}^{6}+1}{\mathrm{y}^{3}}=\mathrm{y}^{3}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{y}^{3}} \\ =\left(\mathrm{y}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{y}}\right)^{3}-3 \cdot \mathrm{y} \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{y}}\left(\mathrm{y}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{y}}\right) \\ =(\sqrt{3})^{3}-3 \cdot \sqrt{3}=3 \sqrt{3}-3 \sqrt{3}=0 \\ \text { বামপক্ষ }=\left(\frac{y^{6}+1}{y^{3}}\right)\left(y^{2}-\frac{1}{y^{2}}\right) \\ =0 .\left(\mathrm{y}^{2}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{y}^{2}}\right)=0=\text { ডানপক্ষ} \\ \therefore \quad\left(\frac{y^{6}+1}{y^{3}}\right)\left(y^{2}-\frac{1}{y^{2}}\right)=0 \text {. (প্রমাণিত) } \end{array} \)
ঘ

Question #7 (ID: 805263)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x+y=\sqrt{7}, x^{2}-y^{2}=\sqrt{35} \text { এবং } p^{2}=5+\sqrt{24.}[/math]আদমজী ক্যান্টনমেন্ট কলেজ, ঢাকা'

Options:
ক. <p>উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর : \( 54 \mathrm{~m}^{4}+27 \mathrm{~m}^{3} \mathrm{a}-16 \mathrm{~m}-8 \mathrm{a} \).</p>

খ. <p>\( 24 x y\left(x^{2}+y^{2}\right) \) এর মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>

গ. <p>প্রমাণ কর যে, \( \mathrm{p}^{5}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{3}}=218 \sqrt{2} \).</p>



Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কধরি, \( f(m)=54 m^{4}+27 m^{3} a-16 m-8 a \)তাহলে, \( f\left(-\frac{1}{2} a\right)=54\left(-\frac{1}{2} a\right)^{4}+27 a\\\left(-\frac{1}{2} a\right)^{3}-16\left(-\frac{1}{2} a\right)-8 a \)\( =\frac{27}{8} a^{4}-\frac{27}{8} a^{4}+8 a-8 a=0 \)\( \therefore \mathrm{m}-\left(-\frac{1}{2} \mathrm{a}\right)=\mathrm{m}+\frac{\mathrm{a}}{2}=\frac{1}{2}(2 \mathrm{~m}+\mathrm{a}), f(\mathrm{~m}) \) এর একটি উৎপাদক অর্থাৎ \( (2 \mathrm{~m}+\mathrm{a}), f(\mathrm{~m}) \) এর একটি উৎপাদক।এখন, \( 54 \mathrm{~m}^{4}+27 \mathrm{~m}^{3} \mathrm{a}-16 \mathrm{~m}-8 \mathrm{a} \)\( =27 \mathrm{~m}^{3}(2 \mathrm{~m}+\mathrm{a})-8(2 m+a) \)\( =(2 \mathrm{~m}+\mathrm{a})\left(27 \mathrm{~m}^{3}-8\right) \)\( =(2 \mathrm{~m}+\mathrm{a})\left\{(3 \mathrm{~m})^{3}-(2)^{3}\right\} \)\( =(2 \mathrm{~m}+\mathrm{a})(3 \mathrm{~m}-2)\left\{(3 \mathrm{~m})^{2}+3 \mathrm{~m} .2+2^{2}\right\} \)\( \left.=(2 m+a)(3 m-2) 9 m^{2}+6 m+4\right) \)নির্ণেয় উৎপাদক : \( (2 \mathrm{~m}+\mathrm{a})(3 \mathrm{~m}-2)\left(9 \mathrm{~m}^{2}+6 \mathrm{~m}+4\right) \)
খদেওয়া আছে, \( x+y=\sqrt{7} \)এবং \( \mathrm{x}^{2}-\mathrm{y}^{2}=\sqrt{35} \)বা, \( (x+y)(x-y)=\sqrt{35} \)বা, \( \sqrt{7}(x-y)=\sqrt{35} \)বা, \( x-y=\frac{\sqrt{7} \cdot \sqrt{5}}{\sqrt{7}} \)\( \therefore \quad \mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y}=\sqrt{5} \)প্রদত্ত রাশি \( =24 x y\left(x^{2}+y^{2}\right)=3.4 x y \cdot 2\left(x^{2}+y^{2}\right) \)[math]=3\left[\{x+y)^2+(x-y)^2\right\} \\\cdot\left\{(x+y)^2+(x-y)^2\right\}[/math][math]\begin{aligned} &amp; =3\left[\left\{(\sqrt{7})^2-(\sqrt{5})^2\right\}\left\{(\sqrt{7})^2+(\sqrt{5})^2\right\}\right] \\ &amp; =3(7-5)(7+5)=3 \times 2 \times 12=72\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় মান: 72
গদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{p}^{2}=5+\sqrt{24} \)বা, \( p^{2}=5+\sqrt{4 \times 6} \)বা, \( p^{2}=5+2 \sqrt{6} \)বা, \( p^{2}=3+2 \sqrt{6}+2 \)বা, \( p^{2}=(\sqrt{3})^{2}+2 \cdot \sqrt{3} \cdot \sqrt{2}+(\sqrt{2})^{2} \)বা, \( p^{2}=(\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2})^{2} \)\( \therefore \quad \mathrm{p}=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2} \)[math]\therefore \frac{1}{p}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}}=\frac{1(\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2})}{(\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2})(\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2})}[math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}}{(\sqrt{3})^2-(\sqrt{2})^2}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}}{3-2}=\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}[/math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \therefore p+\frac{1}{p}=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}+\sqrt{3}-\sqrt{2}=2 \sqrt{3} \\ &amp; p-\frac{1}{p}=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}-\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}=2 \sqrt{2}\end{aligned}[math]\begin{aligned} \text { এখন, } \mathrm{p}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^2} &amp; =\left(\mathrm{p}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}\right)^2-2 \cdot \mathrm{p} \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}} \\ &amp; =(2 \sqrt{3})^2-2=12-2=10\end{aligned}[/math]এবং, [math]\mathrm{p}^3-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^3}=\left(\mathrm{p}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}\right)^3+3 \cdot \mathrm{p} \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}\left(\mathrm{p}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}\right)[/math]=(2 \sqrt{2})^3+3 \cdot 2 \sqrt{2}=16 \sqrt{2}+6 \sqrt{2}=22 \sqrt{2}[/math]বামপক্ষ [math]=p^5-\frac{1}{p^5}[math]=\left(\mathrm{p}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^2}\right)\left(\mathrm{p}^3-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^3}\right)-\left(\mathrm{p}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}\right)[/math]=10 \times 22 \sqrt{2}-2 \sqrt{2}=220 \sqrt{2}-2\\ \sqrt{2}=218 \sqrt{2}= \text {ডানপক্ষ}[/math][math]\therefore \mathrm{p}^5-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^5}=218 \sqrt{2}[/math] (প্রমাণিত)

Question #8 (ID: 805264)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(i) [math]a-2=\frac{1}{a}[/math];

(ii) [math]x^{4}=4\left(4 x^{2}-1\right)[/math]সি. বো.'2022

Options:
ক. <p>উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর : \( x^{2}+4 x-21 \).</p>

খ. <p>প্রমাণ কর যে, \( \mathrm{x}=\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{3} \).</p>

গ. <p>\( \mathrm{a}^{5}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^{5}} \) এর মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>



Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি[math]=x^2+4 x-21[/math][math]\begin{aligned} &amp; =x^2+7 x-3 x-21 \\ &amp; =x(x+7)-3(x+7)=(x+7)(x-3)\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষিত রূপ : \( (x+7)(x-3) \).
খদেওয়া আছে, \( x^{4}=4\left(4 x^{2}-1\right) \)বা, \( x^{4}=16 x^{2}-4 \)বা, \( x^{4}-16 x^{2}+4=0 \)বা, \( \left(x^{2}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot x^{2} .8+8^{2}-8^{2}+4=0 \)বা, \( \left(x^{2}-8\right)^{2}=60 \)বা, \( x^{2}-8=\sqrt{60} \)বা, \( x^{2}-8=\sqrt{4 \times 15} \)বা, \( x^{2}=2 \sqrt{15}+8 \)বা, \( x^{2}=5+2 \sqrt{15}+3 \)বা, \( x^{2}=(\sqrt{5})^{2}+2 \cdot \sqrt{5} \cdot \sqrt{3}+(\sqrt{3})^{2} \)বা, \( x^{2}=(\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{3})^{2} \)\( \therefore \quad x=\sqrt{5}+\sqrt{3} \). (প্রমাণিত)
গদেওয়া আছে, \( a-2=\frac{1}{a} \)বা, \( a-\frac{1}{a}=2 \)&hellip;&hellip;&hellip;.(i)এখন, \( \left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}\\=\left(a-\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}+4 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}=2^{2}+4=4+4=8 \)\( \therefore \quad a+\frac{1}{a}=\sqrt{8} \)এখানে, \( a^{2}+\frac{1}{a^{2}}=\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{2}-2 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}\\=(\sqrt{8})^{2}-2=8-2=6 \)আবার, \( a^{3}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}=\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^{3}-3 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right) \)[math]=(\sqrt{8})^3-3 \times \sqrt{8}=8 \sqrt{8}-3 \sqrt{8}=5 \sqrt{8}[/math][math]\therefore \quad\left(a^2+\frac{1}{a^2}\right)\left(a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}\right)=6 \times 5 \sqrt{8}[/math]বা, \( a^{5}+\frac{1}{a}+a+\frac{1}{a^{5}}=30 \sqrt{8} \)বা, \( \left(a^{5}+\frac{1}{a^{5}}\right)+\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)=30 \sqrt{8} \)বা, \( a^{5}+\frac{1}{a^{5}}+\sqrt{8}=30 \sqrt{8} \)বা, \( a^{5}+\frac{1}{a^{3}}=30 \sqrt{8}-\sqrt{8} \)বা, \( a^{5}+\frac{1}{a^{5}}=29 \sqrt{8}=29 \times 2 \sqrt{2}=58 \sqrt{2} \)নির্ণেয় মান : \( 58 \sqrt{2} \).

Question #9 (ID: 805265)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{p}^{2}=15+4 \sqrt{14}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y}+\mathrm{z}=0[/math].রাজউক উত্তরা মডেল কলেজ, ঢাকা'

Options:
ক. <p>উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর : \( a^{3}-9 b^{3}+(a+b)^{3} \).</p>

খ. <p>\( \mathrm{p}^{3}-\frac{1}{\mathbf{p}^{3}} \) এর মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>

গ. <p>দেখাও যে, \( \frac{(x+y)^{2}}{6 x y}+\frac{(y+z)^{2}}{6 y z}+\frac{(z+x)^{2}}{6 z x}=\frac{1}{2} \).</p>



Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \text { প্রদত্ত রাশি }=a^3-9 b^3+(a+b)^3 \\ &amp; =a^3-b^3+(a+b)^3-8 b^3 \\ &amp; =(a-b)\left(a^2+a b+b^2\right)+(a+b)^3-(2 b)^3\end{aligned}[math]=(\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})\left(\mathrm{a}^2+\mathrm{ab}+\mathrm{b}^2\right)+(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}-2 \mathrm{~b})\\\left\{(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})^2+(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}) 2 \mathrm{~b}+(2 \mathrm{~b})^2\right\}[/math]=(a-b)\left(a^2+a b+b^2\right)+(a-b)\\\left(a^2+2 a b+b^2+2 a b+2 b^2+4 b^2\right)[math]=(a-b)\left(a^2+a b+b^2\right)+(a-b)\\\left(a^2+4 a b+7 b^2\right)[/math]\begin{aligned} &amp; =(a-b)\left(a^2+a b+b^2+a^2+4 a b+7 b^2\right) \\ &amp; =(a-b)\left(2 a^2+5 a b+8 b^2\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, \( \mathrm{p}^{2}=15+4 \sqrt{14} \)বা, \( p^{2}=8+4 \sqrt{14}+7 \)বা, \( p^{2}=(2 \sqrt{2})^{2}+2 \cdot 2 \sqrt{2} \cdot \sqrt{7}+(\sqrt{7})^{2} \)বা, \( p^{2}=(2 \sqrt{2}+\sqrt{7})^{2} \)বা, \( \mathrm{p}=2 \sqrt{2}+\sqrt{7} \)বা, \( \frac{1}{p}=\frac{1}{2 \sqrt{2}+\sqrt{7}} \)বা, \( \frac{1}{p}=\frac{2 \sqrt{2}-\sqrt{7}}{(2 \sqrt{2}+\sqrt{7})(2 \sqrt{2}-\sqrt{7})} \)বা, \( \frac{1}{p}=\frac{2 \sqrt{2}-\sqrt{7}}{(2 \sqrt{2})^{2}-(\sqrt{7})^{2}}=\frac{2 \sqrt{2}-\sqrt{7}}{8-7} \)\( \therefore \frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}=2 \sqrt{2}-\sqrt{7} \)এখন, \( \mathrm{p}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}}=2 \sqrt{2}+\sqrt{7}-(2 \sqrt{2}-\sqrt{7}) \)\( =2 \sqrt{2}+\sqrt{7}-2 \sqrt{2}+\sqrt{7}=2 \sqrt{7} \)প্রদত্ত রাশি \( =\mathrm{p}^{3}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^{3}} \)\( \begin{array}{l} =p^{3}-\left(\frac{1}{p}\right)^{3} \\ =\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)^{3}+3 \cdot p \cdot \frac{1}{p}\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right) \\ =(2 \sqrt{7})^{3}+3.2 \sqrt{7} \\ =8.7 \sqrt{7}+6 \sqrt{7}=56 \sqrt{7}+6 \sqrt{7}=62 \sqrt{7} \end{array} \)নির্ণেয় মান : \( 62 \sqrt{7} \).
গদেওয়া আছে, \( x+y+z=0 \)বা, \( x+y=-z \)এখন, \( x^{3}+y^{3}+z^{3}=(x+y)^{3}-3 . x y(x+y)+z^{3} \)\( \begin{array}{c} \quad(-z)^{3}-3 x y \cdot(-z)+z^{3}[\because x+y=-z] \\ =-z^{3}+3 x y z+z^{3}=3 x y z \\ \therefore x^{3}+y^{3}+z^{3}=3 x y z \\ \text { বামপক্ষ }=\frac{(x+y)^{2}}{6 x y}+\frac{(y+z)^{2}}{6 y z}+\frac{(z+x)^{2}}{6 z x} \\ \quad=\frac{(x+y+z-z)^{2}}{6 x y}+\frac{(x+y+z-x)^{2}}{6 y z}+\frac{(x+y+z-y)^{2}}{6 z x} \end{array} \)[math]=\frac{(0-z)^2}{6 x y}+\frac{(0-x)^2}{6 y z}+\frac{(0-y)^2}{6 z x}[\because x+y+z=0][/math][math]\begin{aligned} &amp; =\frac{z^2}{6 x y}+\frac{x^2}{6 y z}+\frac{y^2}{6 z x} \\ &amp; =\frac{z^3+x^3+y^3}{6 x y z} \\ &amp; =\frac{3 x y z}{6 x y z}\left[\because x^3+y^3+z^3=3 x y z\right] \\ &amp; =\frac{1}{2}\end{aligned}[/math]= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \frac{(x+y)^2}{6 x y}+\frac{(y+z)^2}{6 y z}+\frac{(z+x)^2}{6 z x}=\frac{1}{2}[/math](দেখানো হলো)
ঘ

Question #10 (ID: 805266)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দুইটি বীজগণিতীয় সমীকরণ [math]\mathrm{x}^6+1=18 \sqrt{3} \mathrm{x}^3[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{p}^2=7+4 \sqrt{3}[/math].ঢা. বো.'2022

Options:
ক. [math]y^2+2 z-1-z^2[/math] কে উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{x}=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}[/math].
গ. [math]\frac{p^6-1}{p^3}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি[math]\begin{aligned}\text { } &amp; =y^2+2 z-1-z^2 \\&amp; =y^2-\left(z^2-2 z+1\right)\\&amp;=y^2-\left(z^2-2 \cdot z \cdot 1+1^2\right) \\&amp; =y^2-(z-1)^2=(y+z-1)(y-z+1)\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষিত রূপ : [math](y+z-1)(y-z+1)[/math].
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{x}^6+1=18 \sqrt{3} \mathrm{x}^3[/math]বা, [math]x^6-18 \sqrt{3} x^3+1=0[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^3\right)^2-2 \cdot x^3 \cdot 9 \sqrt{3}+(9 \sqrt{3})^2-(9 \sqrt{3})^2+1=0[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^3-9 \sqrt{3}\right)^2=(9 \sqrt{3})^2-1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^3-9 \sqrt{3}\right)^2=243-1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^3-9 \sqrt{3}\right)^2=242[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^3-9 \sqrt{3}\right)=\sqrt{242}[/math]বা, [math]x^3-9 \sqrt{3}=\sqrt{121 \times 2}[/math]বা, [math]x^3-9 \sqrt{3}=11 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]x^3=11 \sqrt{2}+9 \sqrt{3}[/math]বা, [math]x^3=9 \sqrt{2}+2 \sqrt{2}+3 \sqrt{3}+6 \sqrt{3}[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{x}^3=3 \sqrt{3}+9 \sqrt{2}+6 \sqrt{3}+2 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]x^3=(\sqrt{3})^3+3 \cdot(\sqrt{3})^2 \cdot \sqrt{2}\\+3 \cdot \sqrt{3} \cdot(\sqrt{2})^2+(\sqrt{2})^3[/math]বা, [math]x^3=(\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2})^3[/math][math]\therefore \quad x=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}[/math]. (প্রমাণিত)
গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{p}^2=7+4 \sqrt{3}[/math]বা, [math]\quad {p}^2=4+4 \sqrt{3}+3[/math]বা, [math]p^2=2^2+2 \cdot 2 \cdot \sqrt{3}+(\sqrt{3})^2[/math]বা, [math]p^2=(2+\sqrt{3})^2[/math]বা, [math]p=2+\sqrt{3}[math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \quad \frac{1}{p} &amp; =\frac{1}{2+\sqrt{3}} \\&amp; =\frac{(2-\sqrt{3})}{(2+\sqrt{3})(2-\sqrt{3})}\\&amp; \text {[লব ও হরকে}(2-\sqrt{3}) \text{দ্বারা গুণ করে]} \\&amp; =\frac{2-\sqrt{3}}{2^2-(\sqrt{3})^2}=\frac{2-\sqrt{3}}{4-3}=\frac{2-\sqrt{3}}{1} \\\therefore \quad \frac{1}{p} &amp; =2-\sqrt{3}\end{aligned}[/math]এখানে, [math]\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)=2+\sqrt{3}-(2-\sqrt{3})[/math]=2+\sqrt{3}-2+\sqrt{3}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math]এখন, প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\frac{p^6-1}{p^3}[/math][math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =p^6-\frac{1}{p^3} \\&amp; =p^3-\frac{1}{p^3}=\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)^3+3 \cdot p \cdot \frac{1}{p}\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right) \\&amp; =(2 \sqrt{3})^3+3 \times 2 \sqrt{3} \\&amp; =8 \times 3 \sqrt{3}+6 \sqrt{3} \\&amp; =24 \sqrt{3}+6 \sqrt{3}=30 \sqrt{3}\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় মান:[math]30\sqrt{3}.[/math]
ঘ

Question #11 (ID: 805267)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{x}^4-\mathrm{x}^2+1=0 \text { এবং } \mathrm{p}=18.[/math]য. বো.'2020

Options:
ক. উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর : [math]4 a^2+\frac{1}{4 a^2}-2+4 a-\frac{1}{a}[/math].
খ. [math]\mathrm{x}^5+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^5}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\mathrm{p}=\mathrm{a}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^3}[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{a}=\frac{3+\sqrt{5}}{2}[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক[math]\begin{aligned} \text { প্রদত্ত রাশি } &amp; =4 a^2+\frac{1}{4 a^2}-2+4 a-\frac{1}{a} \\ &amp; =(2 a)^2-2 \cdot 2 a \cdot \frac{1}{2 a}+\left(\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^2\\&amp;+2\left(2 a-\frac{1}{2 a}\right) \\ &amp; =\left(2 a-\frac{1}{2 a}\right)^2+2\left(2 a-\frac{1}{2 a}\right) \\ &amp; =\left(2 a-\frac{1}{2 a}\right)\left(2 a-\frac{1}{2 a}+2\right) .\end{aligned}[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]x^4-x^2+1=0[/math]বা, [math]x^4+1=x^2[/math]বা, [math]\frac{x^4+1}{x^2}=\frac{x^2}{x^2}[/math] [উভয়পক্ষকে [math]x^2[/math] দ্বারা ভাগ করে]বা, [math]\frac{x^4}{x^2}+\frac{1}{x^2}=1[/math]বা, [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-2=1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=1+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=3[math]\begin{aligned}\therefore x+\frac{1}{x} &amp; =\sqrt{3} \\x^3+\frac{1}{x^3} &amp; =\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^3-3 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right) \\&amp; =(\sqrt{3})^3-3 \sqrt{3}=3 \sqrt{3}-3 \sqrt{3}=0\end{aligned}[/math]এখন, [math]\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)\left(\mathrm{x}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^3}\right)=1 \times 0[/math]বা, [math]x^5+x+\frac{1}{x}+\frac{1}{x^5}=0[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}+\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)=0[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}+\sqrt{3}=0[/math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{x}^5+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^5}=-\sqrt{3}[/math]নির্ণেয় মান : [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^3}=-\sqrt{3}[/math].
গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{p}=18[/math].[math]p=a^3+\frac{1}{a^3} \text { হলে, }[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{a}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^3}=18[/math]বা, [math]\frac{a^6+1}{a^3}=18[/math]বা, [math]a^6+1=18 a^3[/math]বা, [math]a^6-18 a^3+1=0[/math]বা, [math]\left(a^3\right)^2-2 \cdot a^3 \cdot 9+9^2-(9)^2+1=0[/math]বা, [math]\left(\mathrm{a}^3-9\right)^2-81+1=0[/math]বা, [math]\left(a^3-9\right)^2=80[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{a}^3-9=\sqrt{80}=\sqrt{16 \times 5}[/math]বা, [math]a^3-9=4 \sqrt{5}[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{a}^3=\frac{27}{8}+\frac{27 \sqrt{5}}{8}+\frac{45}{8}+\frac{5 \sqrt{5}}{8}[/math]বা, [math]a^3=\left(\frac{3}{2}\right)^3+3\left(\frac{3}{2}\right)^2 \cdot \frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}+3 \cdot \frac{3}{2} \cdot\left(\frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}\right)^2\\+\left(\frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}\right)^3[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{a}^3=\left(\frac{3}{2}+\frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}\right)^3[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{a}=\frac{3}{2}+\frac{\sqrt{5}}{2}[/math] [ঘনমূল করে][math]\therefore \quad a=\frac{3+\sqrt{5}}{2}[/math] (প্রমাণিত)

Question #12 (ID: 805268)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p+q=\sqrt{3}, p^2-q^2=\sqrt{6} \text { এবং } A=y^4+\frac{1}{y^4}[/math]ঢা. বো.'2020

Options:
ক. উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর : [math]4 x^2-12 x y+9 y^2-16 z^2[/math].
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{p}^3+\mathrm{q}^3=\frac{9 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math].
গ. [math]\mathrm{A}=\mathrm{m}^4+4 \mathrm{~m}^2+2[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm{y}^2-1=\mathrm{my}[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \text { } 4 x^2-12 x y+9 y^2-16 z^2 \\&amp; =(2 x)^2-2 \cdot 2 x \cdot 3 y+(3 y)^2-(4 z)^2 \\&amp; =(2 x-3 y)^2-(4 z)^2\\&amp;=(2 x-3 y+4 z)(2 x-3 y-4 z)\end{aligned}[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q}=\sqrt{3}[/math]এবং [math]p^2-q^2=\sqrt{6}[/math]বা, [math](p+q)(p-q)=\sqrt{3} \cdot \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]\sqrt{3}(p-q)=\sqrt{3} \cdot \sqrt{2} [\because p+q=\sqrt{3}][math]\therefore \quad p-q=\sqrt{2}[/math]আমরা জানি, [math](p+q)^2=(p-q)^2+4 p q[/math]বা, [math](\sqrt{3})^2=(\sqrt{2})^2+4 \mathrm{pq}[/math]বা, [math]3=2+4 \mathrm{pq}[/math]বা, [math]4 p q=3-2=1[/math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{pq}=\frac{1}{4}[/math]বামপক্ষ [math]=\mathrm{p}^3+\mathrm{q}^3=(\mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q})^3-3 \mathrm{pq}(\mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q})\\=(\sqrt{3})^3-3 \cdot \frac{1}{4} \cdot \sqrt{3}[math]=3 \sqrt{3}-\frac{3 \sqrt{3}}{4}=\frac{12 \sqrt{3}-3 \sqrt{3}}{4}=\frac{9 \sqrt{3}}{4}=\text { ডানপক্ষ }[/math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{p}^3+\mathrm{q}^3=\frac{9 \sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]. (প্রমাণিত)
গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{A}=\mathrm{y}^4+\frac{1}{\mathrm{y}^4}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{A}=\mathrm{m}^4+4 \mathrm{~m}^2+2[/math] এখন, [math]\mathrm{y}^4+\frac{1}{\mathrm{y}^4}=\mathrm{m}^4+4 \mathrm{~m}^2+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(y^2+\frac{1}{y^2}\right)^2-2 \cdot y^2 \cdot \frac{1}{y^2}=m^4+4 m^2+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(y^2+\frac{1}{y^2}\right)^2=m^4+4 m^2+2+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(y^2+\frac{1}{y^2}\right)^2=m^4+4 m^2+4[/math]বা, [math]\left(y^2+\frac{1}{y^2}\right)^2=\left(m^2\right)^2+2 \cdot m^2 \cdot 2+2^2[/math]বা, [math]\left(y^2+\frac{1}{y^2}\right)^2=\left(m^2+2\right)^2[/math] বা, [math]y^2+\frac{1}{y^2}=m^2+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(y-\frac{1}{y}\right)^2+2 \cdot y \cdot \frac{1}{y}=m^2+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(y-\frac{1}{y}\right)^2+2=m^2+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(y-\frac{1}{y}\right)^2=m^2+2-2=m^2[/math]বা, [math]y-\frac{1}{y}=m[/math]বা, [math]\frac{y^2-1}{y}=m[/math].[math]\therefore \quad y^2-1=[/math] my. (দেখানো হলো)
ঘ

Question #13 (ID: 805269)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]b+\frac{1}{b}=5, p^4=119-\frac{1}{p^4}.[/math]চ. বো.'2019

Options:
ক. [math]m^4-7 m^2+1[/math] কে উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{\mathrm{b}^8-1}{\mathrm{~b}^4}=115 \sqrt{21}[/math].
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{p}^6-1-36 \mathrm{p}^3=0[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক[math]\begin{aligned} \text { প্রদত্ত রাশি } &amp; =m^4-7 m^2+1 \\ &amp; =\left(m^2\right)^2+2 m^2 \cdot 1+1^2-9 m^2 \\ &amp; =\left(m^2+1\right)^2-(3 m)^2 \\ &amp; =\left(m^2+1+3 m\right)\left(m^2+1-3 m\right) \\ &amp; =\left(m^2+3 m+1\right)\left(m^2-3 m+1\right) .\end{aligned}[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]b+\frac{1}{b}=5[/math]আমরা জানি, [math]\left(b-\frac{1}{b}\right)^2=\left(b+\frac{1}{b}\right)^2-4 b \cdot \frac{1}{b}\\=5^2-4=25-4=21[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \therefore b-\frac{1}{b}=\sqrt{21} \\&amp; \text { এখন, } b^2+\frac{1}{b^2}=\left(b+\frac{1}{b}\right)^2-2 b \cdot \frac{1}{b}\\&amp;=5^2-2=25-2=23 \\&amp; \therefore b^2-\frac{1}{b^2}=\left(b+\frac{1}{b}\right)\left(b-\frac{1}{b}\right)\\&amp;=5 \times \sqrt{21}=5 \sqrt{21}\end{aligned}[/math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \text { বামপক্ষ }=\frac{b^8-1}{b^4}=\frac{b^8}{b^4}-\frac{1}{b^4}=b^4-\frac{1}{b^4}\\&amp;=\left(b^2\right)^2-\left(\frac{1}{b^2}\right)^2 \\ &amp; \quad=\left(b^2+\frac{1}{b^2}\right)\left(b^2-\frac{1}{b^2}\right)\\&amp;=23 \times 5 \sqrt{21}=115 \sqrt{21}=\text { ডানপক্ষ } \\ &amp; \therefore \frac{b^8-1}{b^4}=115 \sqrt{21} \text {. (প্রমাণিত) }\end{aligned}[/math]
গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{p}^4=119-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^4}[/math]বা, [math]p^4+\frac{1}{p^4}=119[/math]বা, [math]\left(p^2\right)^2+\left(\frac{1}{p^2}\right)^2=119[/math].বা, [math]\left(p^2+\frac{1}{p^2}\right)^2-2 p^2 \cdot \frac{1}{p^2}=119[/math]বা, [math]\left(p^2+\frac{1}{p^2}\right)^2=119+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(p^2+\frac{1}{p^2}\right)^2=121[/math]বা, [math]p^2+\frac{1}{p^2}=\sqrt{121}[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{p}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^2}=11[/math]বা, [math]\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)^2+2 p \cdot \frac{1}{p}=11[/math]বা, [math]\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)^2=11-2[/math]বা, [math]\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)^2=9[/math]বা, [math]p-\frac{1}{p}=\sqrt{9}[/math]বা, [math]p-\frac{1}{p}=3[/math]বা, [math]\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)^3=3^3[/math]বা, [math]p^3-3 p^2 \cdot \frac{1}{p}+3 p \cdot \frac{1}{p^2}-\frac{1}{p^3}=27[/math]বা, [math]p^3-\frac{1}{p^3}-3\left(p-\frac{1}{p}\right)=27[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{p}^3-\frac{1}{\mathrm{p}^3}-3 \times 3=27=27+9[/math]বা, [math]\frac{p^6-1}{p^3}=36[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{p}^6-1=36 \mathrm{p}^3[/math][math]\therefore \quad p^6-1-36 p^3=0[/math]. (প্রমাণিত)
ঘ

Question #14 (ID: 805270)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
একটি ধনাত্মক সংখ্যার বর্গ ঐ সংখ্যার পাঁচগুণ হতে [math]1[/math] কম।ঢা. বো.'2015

Options:
ক. ধনাত্মক সংখ্যাটি [math]x[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}=5[/math].
খ. [math]\mathrm{x}^3-\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^3}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}=2525[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কধরি, ধনাত্মক সংখ্যাটি [math]x[math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{x}[/math] এর বর্গ [math]=\mathrm{x}^2[/math]x[/math] এর পাঁচগুণ [math]=5 \times \mathrm{x}=5 \mathrm{x}[/math]শর্তমতে, [math]\mathrm{x}^2=5 \mathrm{x}-1[/math]বা, [math]x^2+1=5 x[/math]বা, [math]x\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)=5 x[/math]বা, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=\frac{5 x}{x}[/math][math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}=5[/math]. (দেখানো হলো)
খ'ক' হতে, [math]\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}=5[/math]এখন, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}[math]=5^2-4=25-4=21[/math]\therefore \quad x-\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{21}[/math]প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=x^3-\frac{1}{x^3}[/math][math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^3+3 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right) \\&amp; =(\sqrt{21})^3+3 \cdot \sqrt{21} \\&amp; =21 \sqrt{21}+3 \sqrt{21}=24 \sqrt{21}\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় মান [math]24 \sqrt{21}[/math].
গ'ক' হতে, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=5[/math]এখন, [math]\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}=\left(\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\right)^2-2 \cdot \mathrm{x} \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}[math]=5^2-2=25-2=23[/math]এবং [math]\mathrm{x}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^3}=\left(\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\right)^3-3 \cdot \mathrm{x} \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\left(\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\right)[/math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =5^3-3 \times 5 \\&amp; =125-15=110\end{aligned}[/math]এখন, [math]\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)\left(\mathrm{x}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^3}\right)=23 \times 110[/math]বা, [math]x^5+x+\frac{1}{x}+\frac{1}{x^5}=2530[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}+\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)=2530[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}+5=2530[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^3}=2530-5[/math][math]\therefore \quad x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}=2525[/math]. (প্রমাণিত)
ঘ

Question #15 (ID: 805271)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(i) [math]x^4-38 x^2+1=0[/math] [যখন [math]x&gt;0[/math] ]

(ii) [math]\mathrm{a}^2=17+12 \sqrt{2}[/math] [যখন [math]\mathrm{a}&gt;0[/math] ]ঢা. বো.'2023

Options:
ক. উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর : [math]4 \mathrm{P}^2-1+2 \mathrm{R}-\mathrm{R}^2[/math].
খ. (i) এর সাহায্যে [math]\frac{x^8-1}{x^4}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. (ii) এর সাহায্যে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]a^5+\frac{1}{a^5}=6726[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক[math]\begin{aligned} \text { প্রদত্ত রাশি } &amp; =4 \mathrm{P}^2-1+2 \mathrm{R}-\mathrm{R}^2 \\ &amp; =4 \mathrm{P}^2-\left(\mathrm{R}^2-2 \mathrm{R}+1\right) \\ &amp; =4 \mathrm{P}^2-(\mathrm{R}-1)^2 \\ &amp; =(2 \mathrm{P})^2-(\mathrm{R}-1)^2\\&amp;=(2 \mathrm{P}+\mathrm{R}-1)(2 \mathrm{P}-\mathrm{R}+1)\end{aligned}[/math]
খ(i) নং হতে পাই, [math]x^4-38 x^2+1=0 ; x&gt;0[/math]বা, [math]x^4+1=38 x^2[/math]বা, [math]\frac{x^4}{x^2}+\frac{1}{x^2}=\frac{38 x^2}{x^2}[/math] [উভয়পক্ষকে [math]x^2[/math] দ্বারা ভাগ করে]বা, [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=38 \ldots \ldots \ldots(i)[/math]বা, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2+2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=38[/math]বা, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2+2=38[/math]বা, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=38-2[/math].বা, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=36[/math]বা, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=6^2[math]\therefore \quad x-\frac{1}{x}=6 \ldots \ldots\ldots (ii)[/math]আমরা জানি,[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \quad\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2+4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=6^2+4\\&amp;=36+4=40 \\&amp; \therefore \quad x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{40}=2 \sqrt{10} \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (iii) }\end{aligned}[/math]প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\frac{x^8-1}{x^4}[/math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =\frac{x^8}{x^4}-\frac{1}{x^4}=x^4-\frac{1}{x^4} \\&amp; =\left(x^2\right)^2-\left(\frac{1}{x^2}\right)^2=\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)\left(x^2-\frac{1}{x^2}\right) \\&amp; =\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right) \\&amp; =38 \times 2 \sqrt{10} \times 6[(\mathrm{i}),(\mathrm{ii}) \text { ও (iii) নং হতে মান বসিয়ে }] \\&amp; =456 \sqrt{10}\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় মান : [math]456 \sqrt{10}[/math].
গ(ii) নং হতে পাই,[math]a^2=17+12 \sqrt{2} ; a&gt;0[/math]বा, [math]a^2=9+12 \sqrt{2}+8[/math]বা, [math]a^2=3^2+2 \cdot 3 \cdot 2 \sqrt{2}+(2 \sqrt{2})^2[/math]বা, [math]\mathrm{a}^2=(3+2 \sqrt{2})^2[math]\therefore \quad a=3+2 \sqrt{2} \quad[/math] [বর্গমূল করে][math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \begin{aligned}\therefore \quad \frac{1}{a} &amp; =\frac{1}{3+2 \sqrt{2}} \\&amp; =\frac{3-2 \sqrt{2}}{(3+2 \sqrt{2})(3-2 \sqrt{2})}\\&amp;[\text { লব ও হরকে }(3-2 \sqrt{2}) \text { দ্বারা গুণ করে }] \\&amp; =\frac{3-2 \sqrt{2}}{3^2-(2 \sqrt{2})^2}=\frac{3-2 \sqrt{2}}{9-8}=3-2 \sqrt{2}\end{aligned} \\&amp; \begin{aligned}\therefore a &amp; +\frac{1}{a}=3+2 \sqrt{2}+3-2 \sqrt{2}=6 \\a^2+\frac{1}{a^2} &amp; =\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^2-2 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}\\&amp;=6^2-2=36-2=34\end{aligned}\end{aligned}[/math]আবার, [math]a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}=\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^3-3 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)[/math]=6^3-3 \times 6=216-18=198[/math]বামপক্ষ [math]=a^5+\frac{1}{a^5}[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =\left(a^2+\frac{1}{a^2}\right)\left(a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}\right)-\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right) \\&amp; =34 \times 198-6 \\&amp; =6732-6=6726=\text { ডানপক্ষ }\end{aligned}[/math]\therefore a^5+\frac{1}{a^5}=6726[/math] (প্রমাণিত)
ঘ

Question #16 (ID: 805272)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags:

Question:
[math](l+\mathrm{m})^2=\sqrt[3]{125},(l-\mathrm{m})^2=\sqrt[3]{64}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{k}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{k}^2}=\frac{85}{4} ;[/math] যেখানে [math]\mathrm{k}&gt;0[/math]রা. বো.'2022

Options:
ক. [math]9 c^2+\frac{1}{9 c^2}-2+9 c-\frac{1}{c}[/math] কে উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর (য, [math]4\left(l^3 \mathrm{~m}+l \mathrm{~m}^3\right)=\frac{9}{2}[/math].
গ. দেখাও যে, [math]8\left(\mathrm{k}^3-\frac{1}{\mathrm{k}^3}\right)=89 \sqrt{77}[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি[math]\begin{aligned}\text { } &amp; =9 c^2+\frac{1}{9 c^2}-2+9 c-\frac{1}{c} \\&amp; =(3 c)^2-2 \cdot 3 c \cdot \frac{1}{3 c}+\left(\frac{1}{3 c}\right)^2+3\left(3 c-\frac{1}{3 c}\right) \\&amp; =\left(3 c-\frac{1}{3 c}\right)^2+3\left(3 c-\frac{1}{3 c}\right) \\&amp; =\left(3 c-\frac{1}{3 c}\right)\left(3 c-\frac{1}{3 c}+3\right)\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষিত রূপ : [math]\left(3 c-\frac{1}{3 c}\right)\left(3 c-\frac{1}{3 c}+3\right)[/math].
খদেওয়া আছে, [math](l+m)^2=\sqrt[3]{125}[/math]বা, [math](l+\mathrm{m})^2=\left(5^3\right)^{\frac{1}{3}}=5[/math] [math].........(i)[/math]এবং [math](l-\mathrm{m})^2=\sqrt[3]{64}[/math]বা, [math](l-m)^2=\left(4^3\right)^{\frac{1}{3}}=4[/math] [math]..........(ii)[/math](i)নং হতে (ii)নং বিয়োগ করে পাই,[math](l+\mathrm{m})^2-(l-\mathrm{m})^2=5-4[/math]বা, [math]4 l\operatorname {m}=1\left[\because(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})^2-(\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})^2=4 \mathrm{ab}\right][/math]আবার, (i) ও (ii)নং যোগ করে পাই,[math](l+\mathrm{m})^2+(l-\mathrm{m})^2=5+4[/math]বা, [math]2\left(l^2+m^2\right)=9\left[\because(a+b)^2+(a-b)^2\\=2\left(a^2+b^2\right)\right][/math]বা, [math]l^2+\mathrm{m}^2=\frac{9}{2}[/math]বামপক্ষ [math]=4\left(l^3 \mathrm{~m}+l \mathrm{~m}^3\right)[math]=4l \operatorname{m}\left(l^2+\mathrm{m}^2\right)=1 \times \frac{9}{2}=\frac{9}{2}=\text { ডানপক্ষ }[/math]\therefore \quad 4\left(l^3 \mathrm{~m}+l \mathrm{~m}^3\right)=\frac{9}{2}[/math]. (প্রমাণিত)
গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{k}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{k}^2}=\frac{85}{4}[/math]; যেখানে, [math]\mathrm{k}&gt;0[/math]বা, [math]\left(k-\frac{1}{k}\right)^2+2 \cdot k \cdot \frac{1}{k}=\frac{85}{4}[/math]বা, [math]\left(k-\frac{1}{k}\right)^2+2=\frac{85}{4}[/math]বা, [math]\left(k-\frac{1}{k}\right)^2=\frac{85}{4}-2[/math]বা, [math]\left(k-\frac{1}{k}\right)^2=\frac{85-8}{4}[/math]বা, [math]\left(k-\frac{1}{k}\right)^2=\frac{77}{4}[math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{k}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{k}}=\frac{\sqrt{77}}{2}[/math]বামপক্ষ [math]=8\left(k^3-\frac{1}{k^3}\right)\\=8\left\{\left(k-\frac{1}{k}\right)^3+3 \cdot k \cdot \frac{1}{k}\left(k-\frac{1}{k}\right)\right\}[/math]=8\left\{\left(\frac{\sqrt{77}}{2}\right)^3+3 \times \frac{\sqrt{77}}{2}\right\}=8\left(\frac{77 \sqrt{77}}{8}+\frac{3 \sqrt{77}}{2}\right)[/math][math]=8\left(\frac{77 \sqrt{77}+12 \sqrt{77}}{8}\right)=89 \sqrt{77}=[/math] ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad 8\left(\mathrm{k}^3-\frac{1}{\mathrm{k}^3}\right)=89 \sqrt{77}[/math]. (দেখানো হলো)

Question #17 (ID: 805273)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\left(p^2+q^2\right)^2=\sqrt[3]{125},\left(p^2-q^2\right)^2=\sqrt[3]{64}[/math] এবং [math]x^2=9+4 \sqrt{5}.[/math]ব. বো.'2019

Options:
ক. [math]x^2-2\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right) x+4[/math] কে উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]16\left(p^4+q^4\right) p^2 q^2=18[/math].
গ. [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি[math]\begin{aligned} \text { } &amp; =x^2-2\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right) x+4=x^2-2 a x-\frac{2 x}{a}+4 \\ &amp; =x(x-2 a)-\frac{2}{a}(x-2 a)=(x-2 a)\left(x-\frac{2}{a}\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\left(p^2+q^2\right)^2=\sqrt[3]{125}[/math]বা, [math]\left(p^2+q^2\right)^2=\left(5^3\right)^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]বা, [math]\left(p^2+q^2\right)^2=5[/math]বা, [math]p^2+q^2=\sqrt{5}[/math]এবং [math]\left(p^2-q^2\right)^2=\sqrt[3]{64}[/math]বা, [math]\left(p^2-q^2\right)^2=\left(4^3\right)^{\frac{1}{3}}[/math]বা, [math]\left(p^2-q^2\right)^2=4[/math]বা, [math]p^2-q^2=\sqrt{4}[math]\therefore \quad p^2-q^2=2[/math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \text { বামপক্ষ }=16\left(\mathrm{p}^4+\mathrm{q}^4\right) \mathrm{p}^2 \mathrm{q}^2 \\&amp; =2 \times 4 \mathrm{p}^2 \mathrm{q}^2 \times 2\left(\mathrm{p}^4+\mathrm{q}^4\right)\\&amp;=2 \times 4 \mathrm{p}^2 \mathrm{q}^2 \times 2\left\{\left(\mathrm{p}^2\right)^2+\left(\mathrm{q}^2\right)^2\right\} \\&amp;=2\left\{\left(\mathrm{p}^2+\mathrm{q}^2\right)^2-\left(\mathrm{p}^2-\mathrm{q}^2\right)\right\}\left\{\left(\mathrm{p}^2+\mathrm{q}^2\right)^2 \\+\left(\mathrm{p}^2-\mathrm{q}^2\right)^2\right\} \\&amp; =2\left\{(\sqrt{5})^2-2^2\right\}\left\{(\sqrt{5})^2+2^2\right\} \\&amp; =2(5-4)(5+4)=2 \times 1 \times 9=18=\text { ডানপক্ষ } \\&amp; \therefore \quad 16\left(\mathrm{p}^4+\mathrm{q}^4\right) \mathrm{p}^2 \mathrm{q}^2=18 \text {. (প্রমাণিত) }\end{aligned}[/math]
গদেওয়া আছে, [math]x^2=9+4 \sqrt{5}[/math]বা, [math]x^2=5+4 \sqrt{5}+4[/math]বা, [math]x^2=(\sqrt{5})^2+2 \cdot \sqrt{5} \cdot 2+2^2[/math]বা, [math]x^2=(\sqrt{5}+2)^2[math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{x}=\sqrt{5}+2[/math]আবার, [math]x=\sqrt{5}+2[/math]বা, [math]\frac{1}{x}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{5}+2}[/math]বা, [math]\frac{1}{x}=\frac{1 \times(\sqrt{5}-2)}{(\sqrt{5}+2)(\sqrt{5}-2)}[/math]বा, [math]\frac{1}{x}=\frac{\sqrt{5}-2}{(\sqrt{5})^2-(2)^2}=\frac{\sqrt{5}-2}{5-4}=\sqrt{5}-2[/math]এখন, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{5}+2+\sqrt{5}-2=2 \sqrt{5}[/math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \quad x^2+\frac{1}{x^2} &amp; =\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-2 x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\\&amp;=(2 \sqrt{5})^2-2=20-2=18 \\\therefore \quad x^3+\frac{1}{x^3} &amp; =\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^3-3 x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right) \\&amp; =(2 \sqrt{5})^3-3 \times 2 \sqrt{5}\\&amp;=40 \sqrt{5}-6 \sqrt{5}=34 \sqrt{5}\end{aligned}[/math]প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\mathrm{x}^5+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^5}[/math][math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^3}\right)-\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right) \\&amp; =18 \times 34 \sqrt{5}-2 \sqrt{5}=612 \sqrt{5}-2 \sqrt{5}=610 \sqrt{5}\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় মান [math]610 \sqrt{5}[/math].
ঘ

Question #18 (ID: 805274)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোনো সংখ্যা ও ঐ সংখ্যার গুণাত্মক বিপরীত সংখ্যার সমষ্টি [math]2\sqrt{3}[/math]।রা. বো.'2017

Options:
ক. সংখ্যাটিকে a চলকে প্রকাশ করে উপরের তথ্যকে একটি সমীকরণের মাধ্যমে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. [math]a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}[/math]&nbsp;এর এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]a=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}.[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কধরি, সংখ্যাটি [math] a[/math][math]a[/math] এর গুণাত্মক বিপরীত সংখ্যা [math]=\frac{1}{a}[/math]শর্তমতে, [math]a+\frac{1}{a}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math]নির্ণেয় সমীকরণ, [math]a+\frac{1}{a}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math].
খক-হতে প্রাপ্ত, [math]a+\frac{1}{a}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math]প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}=\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^3-3 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a} \cdot\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)[/math][math]=(2 \sqrt{3})^3-3.2 \sqrt{3}=8.3 \sqrt{3}-6 \sqrt{3}\\=24 \sqrt{3}-6 \sqrt{3}=18 \sqrt{3}[/math]নির্ণেয় মান [math]18 \sqrt{3}[/math].
গক-হতে প্রাপ্ত, [math]a+\frac{1}{a}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math]বা, [math]\frac{a^2+1}{a}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math]বা, [math]a^2+1=2 \sqrt{3} a[/math]বা, [math]a^2-2 \sqrt{3} a+1=0[/math]বা, [math]a^2-2 \cdot a \cdot \sqrt{3}+(\sqrt{3})^2-2=0[/math]বা, [math](a-\sqrt{3})^2-2=0[/math]বা, [math](a-\sqrt{3})^2=2[/math]বা, [math]a-\sqrt{3}=\sqrt{2}[/math][math]\therefore \quad a=\sqrt{3}+\sqrt{2}[/math]. (প্রমাণিত)

Question #19 (ID: 805275)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(i) [math]\mathrm{a}^4=527-\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^4}[/math], যেখানে, [math]\mathrm{a}&gt;0[/math];

(ii) [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=4[/math], যেখানে [math]x&gt;0[/math].রা. বো.'2023

Options:
ক. [math]x^2+10 x+16-y^2+6 y[/math] কে উৎপাদকে বিশ্লেষণ কর।
খ. (i)নং হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{a}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^3}=110[/math].
গ. (ii)নং হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{\mathrm{x}^8-1}{\mathrm{x}^4}=112 \sqrt{3}[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =x^2+10 x+16-y^2+6 y \\&amp; =x^2+10 x+25-y^2+6 y-9 \\&amp; =x^2+2 \cdot x \cdot 5+5^2-\left(y^2-2 \cdot y \cdot 3+3^2\right) \\&amp; =(x+5)^2-(y-3)^2 \\&amp; =(x+5+y-3)(x+5-y+3) \\&amp; =(x+y+2)(x-y+8)\end{aligned}[/math]
খ(i) নং হতে, দেওয়া আছে,[math]a^4=527-\frac{1}{a^4}[/math], যেখানে, [math]a&gt;0[/math]বা, [math]a^4+\frac{1}{a^4}=527[/math]বা, [math]\left(a^2\right)^2+\left(\frac{1}{a^2}\right)^2=527[/math]বা, [math]\left(a^2+\frac{1}{a^2}\right)^2-2 \cdot a^2 \cdot \frac{1}{a^2}=527[/math]বা, [math]\left(a^2+\frac{1}{a^2}\right)^2=527+2[/math]বা, [math]a^2+\frac{1}{a^2}=\sqrt{529}[/math]বা, [math]a^2+\frac{1}{a^2}=23[/math]বা, [math]\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^2-2 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}=23[/math]বা, [math]\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^2-2=23[/math]বা, [math]\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^2=23+2[/math]বা, [math]a+\frac{1}{a}=\sqrt{25}=5[math]\therefore \quad a+\frac{1}{a}=5[/math]বামপক্ষ [math]=a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}[/math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^3-3 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right) \\&amp; =(5)^3-3.5=125-15=110=\text { ডানপক্ষ }\end{aligned}[/math][math]\therefore \quad a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}=110[/math]. (দেখানো হলো)
গ(ii) নং হতে, দেওয়া আছে, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=4[/math], যেখানে [math]x&gt;0[/math].আমরা জানি, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}[/math]বা, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=(4)^2-4=16-4=12[/math]বা, [math]x-\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{12}=\sqrt{4 \times 3}[math]\therefore \quad x-\frac{1}{x}=2 \sqrt{3}[/math]এখন, [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2+2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}[/math]=(4)^2-2=16-2=14[/math]বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{x^8-1}{x^4}=\frac{x^8}{x^4}-\frac{1}{x^4}=x^4-\frac{1}{x^4}[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =\left(x^2\right)^2-\left(\frac{1}{x^2}\right)^2=\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)\left(x^2-\frac{1}{x^2}\right) \\&amp; =\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right) \\&amp; =14 \times 4 \times 2 \sqrt{3}=112 \sqrt{3}=\text { ডানপক্ষ }\end{aligned}[/math]\therefore \quad \frac{x^8-1}{x^4}=112 \sqrt{3}[/math]. (প্রমাণিত)
ঘ

Question #20 (ID: 805276)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]a^4-27 a^2+1=0[/math] এবং [math]x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}=34 \sqrt{5}[/math], যেখানে [math]a, x&gt;0[/math].রা. বো.'2020

Options:
ক. [math]B=\left\{x: x \in Z\right.[/math] এবং [math]\left.x^2&lt;4\right\}[/math] সেটটিকে তালিকা পদ্ধতিতে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. [math]a^4-\frac{1}{a^4}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{x}=2+\sqrt{5}[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{B}=\left\{\mathrm{x}: \mathrm{x} \in \mathrm{Z}\right.[/math] এবং [math]\left.\mathrm{x}^2&lt;4\right\}[/math]অর্থাৎ যেসব পূর্ণসংখ্যার বর্গ 4 অপেক্ষা ছোট তাদের সেট।[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; x=0 \text { হলে, } x^2=0^2=0&lt;4 \\&amp; x= \pm 1 \text { হলে, } x^2=( \pm 1)^2=1&lt;4 \\&amp; x= \pm 2 \text { হলে, } x^2=( \pm 2)^2=4 
less 4\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় সেট, [math]\mathrm{B}=\{-1,0,1\}[/math].
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]a^4-27 a^2+1=0[/math] যেখানে, [math]a&gt;0[/math]বা, [math]a^4+1=27 a^2[/math]বা, [math]\frac{a^4+1}{a^2}=\frac{27 a^2}{a^2}[/math] [উভয়পক্ষে [math]a^2[/math] দ্বারা ভাগ করে]বা, [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}^4}{\mathrm{a}^2}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^2}=27[/math]বা, [math]a^2+\frac{1}{a^2}=27[/math]বা, [math]\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^2-2 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}=27[/math]বা, [math]\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^2-2=27[/math]বা, [math]\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^2=27+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^2=29[/math][math]\therefore \quad a+\frac{1}{a}=\sqrt{29}[/math]
গবা, [math]\left(x^3\right)^2-2 \cdot x^3 \cdot 17 \sqrt{5}\\+(17 \sqrt{5})^2-(17 \sqrt{5})^2+1=0[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^3-17 \sqrt{5}\right)^2-1445+1=0[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^3-17 \sqrt{5}\right)^2-1444=0[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^3-17 \sqrt{5}\right)^2=1444[/math]বা, [math]x^3-17 \sqrt{5}=\sqrt{1444}[/math] [বর্গমূল করে]বা, [math]x^3-17 \sqrt{5}=38[/math]বা, [math]x^3=38-17 \sqrt{5}[/math]বা, [math]x^3=8+12 \sqrt{5}+30+5 \sqrt{5}[/math]বা, [math]x^3=2^3+3 \cdot 2^2 \cdot \sqrt{5}+3 \cdot 2(\sqrt{5})^2+(\sqrt{5})^3[/math]বা, [math]x^3=(2+\sqrt{5})^3[/math]বা, [math]x=2+\sqrt{5}[/math] [ঘনমূল করে][math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{x}=2+\sqrt{5}[/math]. (প্রমাণিত)
ঘ

Question #21 (ID: 805277)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x^2-3=2 \sqrt{2} \text { হলে, }[/math]দি. বো.'2017

Options:
ক. [math]x[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]x^4+\frac{1}{x^4}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{x}^5+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^5}=58 \sqrt{2}[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]x^2-3=2 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]x^2=3+2 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]x^2=2+2 \sqrt{2}+1[/math]বা, [math]x^2=(\sqrt{2})^2+2 \cdot \sqrt{2} \cdot 1+1^2=(\sqrt{2}+1)^2[/math][math]\therefore \quad x= \pm(\sqrt{2}+1)[/math]নির্ণেয় মান : [math]\pm(\sqrt{2}+1)[/math].
খক হতে পাই, [math]x=\sqrt{2}+1[/math] [ধনাত্মক মান নিয়ে]বা, [math]\frac{1}{x}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}+1}[/math]বা, [math]\frac{1}{x}=\frac{(\sqrt{2}-1)}{(\sqrt{2}+1)(\sqrt{2}-1)}=\frac{\sqrt{2}-1}{2-1}=\sqrt{2}-1[math]\therefore \quad x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{2}+1+\sqrt{2}-1=2 \sqrt{2}[/math]প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=x^4+\frac{1}{x^4}[/math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =\left(x^2\right)^2+\left(\frac{1}{x^2}\right)^2 \\&amp; =\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)^2-2 \cdot x^2 \cdot \frac{1}{x^2} \\&amp; =\left\{\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\right\}^2-2 \\&amp; =\left\{(2 \sqrt{2})^2-2\right\}^2-2 \\&amp; =(8-2)^2-2=36-2=34\end{aligned}[/math]নির্ণেয় মান [math]34.[/math]
গখ হতে পাই, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=2 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=(2 \sqrt{2})^2[/math] [বর্গ করে]বা, [math]x^2+2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}+\frac{1}{x^2}=8[/math]বা, [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=8-2[math]\therefore \quad x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=6[/math]আবার, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=2 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^3=(2 \sqrt{2})^3[/math] [ঘন করে]বা, [math]x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}+3 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)=16 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}+3 \cdot 2 \cdot \sqrt{2}=16 \sqrt{2}\left[\because x+\frac{1}{x}=2 \sqrt{2}\right][/math]বা, [math]x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}=16 \sqrt{2}-6 \sqrt{2}[/math]\therefore \quad x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}=10 \sqrt{2}[/math]এখন, [math]\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)\left(x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}\right)=6 \times 10 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x}+x+\frac{1}{x^5}=60 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}+x+\frac{1}{x}=60 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}+2 \sqrt{2}=60 \sqrt{2}[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}=60 \sqrt{2}-2 \sqrt{2}[/math][math]\therefore \quad x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}=58 \sqrt{2}[/math]. (প্রমাণিত)
ঘ

Question #22 (ID: 805278)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x ^ 4 - x ^ 2 + 1 = 0[/math] হলে-য. বো.'2015

Options:
ক. [math]x+\frac{1}{x}[/math] এর মান কত?
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{x^6+1}{x^3}=0[/math].
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}=-\sqrt{3}[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]x^4-x^2+1=0[/math]বা, [math]x^4+1=x^2[/math]বা, [math]x^2\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)=\dot{x}^2[/math]বা, [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=\frac{x^2}{x^2}[/math]বা, [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-2=1[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=1+2[/math]বা, [math]\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=3[/math]বা, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}= \pm \sqrt{3}[/math]নির্ণেয় মান [math]\pm \sqrt{3}[/math].
খক-হতে প্রাপ্ত, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}= \pm \sqrt{3}[/math]বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{x^6+1}{x^3}=x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^3-3 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right) \\&amp; =(\sqrt{3})^3-3 \cdot \sqrt{3}\left[x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{3} \text { বসিয়ে }\right] \\&amp; =3 \sqrt{3}-3 \sqrt{3}=0=\text { ডানপক্ষ }\end{aligned}[/math]\therefore \quad \frac{x^6+1}{x^3}=0[/math]. (দেখানো হলো)
গক-হতে প্রাপ্ত, [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=1[/math]এবং [math]x+\frac{1}{x}= \pm \sqrt{3}[/math]খ-হতে প্রাপ্ত, [math]\mathrm{x}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^3}=0[/math]এখন, [math]\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)\left(\mathrm{x}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^3}\right)=1 \times 0[/math]বা, [math]x^5+x+\frac{1}{x}+\frac{1}{x^5}=0[/math].বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}+\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)=0[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^3}+\sqrt{3}=0\left[x+\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{3}\right.[/math] নিয়ে[math]][/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^3}=-\sqrt{3}[/math].[math]\therefore \quad x^5+\frac{1}{x^3}=-\sqrt{3}[/math].(প্রমাণিত)
ঘ

Question #23 (ID: 805279)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]x-\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{3}[/math] যেখানে [math]x 
eq 0[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x^2-\sqrt{3} x=1[/math]
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]23\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)=5\left(\mathrm{x}^4+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^4}\right)[/math]
গ. [math]x^6+\frac{1}{x^6}[/math]&nbsp;এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]x-\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{3}[/math] যেখানে [math]x 
eq 0[/math]বা, [math]\frac{x^2-1}{x}=\sqrt{3}[/math] বা, [math]x^2-1=\sqrt{3} x \therefore x^2-\sqrt{3} x=1[/math](প্রমাণিত)
খ[math]\begin{aligned} &amp; \mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}=\left(\mathrm{x}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\right)^2+2 \cdot \mathrm{x} \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\\&amp;=(\sqrt{3})^2+2=3+2=5 \\ &amp; \therefore \text { বামপক্ষ }=23\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)=23 \times 5=115 \\ &amp; \text { ডানপক্ষ }=5\left(\mathrm{x}^4+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^4}\right)=5\left\{\left(\mathrm{x}^2\right)^2+\left(\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)^2\right\} \\ &amp; =5\left\{\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)^2-2 \cdot \mathrm{x}^2 \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right\} \\ &amp; =5\left(5^2-2\right)=5(25-2)=5 \times 23=115 \\ &amp; \therefore 23\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)=5\left(\mathrm{x}^4+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^4}\right) \text { (প্রমাণিত) }\end{aligned}[/math]
গ'খ' হতে প্রাপ্ত, [math]\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}=5[/math]প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\mathrm{x}^6+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^6}=\left(\mathrm{x}^2\right)^3+\left(\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)^3[/math] [math]=\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)^3-3 \cdot x^2 \cdot \frac{1}{x^2}\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)[/math] [math]=5^3-3 \times 5=125-15=110[/math] (Ans.)
ঘ

Question #24 (ID: 805280)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোনো সমিতির সদস্যগণ প্রত্যেকেই সদস্য সংখ্যার 100 গুণ চাঁদা দেওয়ার সিদ্ধান্ত নিলেন। কিন্তু 4 জন সদস্য চাঁদা না দেওয়ায় প্রত্যেকের চাঁদার পরিমাণ পূর্বের চেয়ে 500 টাকা বেড়ে গেল।

Options:
ক. সমিতির সদস্য সংখ্যা x এবং মোট চাঁদার পরিমাণ A হলে, এদের মধ্যে সম্পর্ক নির্ণয় কর।
খ. সমিতির সদস্য সংখ্যা ও মোট চাঁদার পরিমাণ নির্ণয় কর।
গ. মোট চাঁদার&nbsp;[math]\frac{1}{4}[/math]&nbsp;অংশ&nbsp;5% হারে এবং অবশিষ্ট টাকা 4% হারে&nbsp;2 বছরের জন্য সরল মুনাফায় বিনিয়োগ করা হলো। মোট মুনাফা নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কএখানে, সমিতির সদস্য সংখ্যা [math]\mathrm x[/math] এবং মোট চাঁদার পরিমাণ[math]\mathrm A[/math]প্রত্যেকের চাঁদার পরিমাণ [math]= 100 &times; \mathrm x[/math] টাকা [math]= 100\mathrm x[/math] টাকা[math]\therefore[/math][math]\mathrm x[/math] জনের চাঁদার পরিমাণ [math]= (100\mathrm x &times; \mathrm x)[/math] টাকা [math]= 100\mathrm x&sup2;[/math] টাকাতাহলে, নির্ণেয় সম্পর্ক, [math]\mathrm A = 100x&sup2;[/math] (Ans.)
খ4 জন সদস্য চাঁদা না দেওয়ায়, ( [math]\mathrm{x}-4[/math] ) জনের প্রত্যেকের চাঁদার পরিমাণ হবে [math](100 \mathrm{x}+500)[/math] টাকা।প্রশ্নমতে, [math](x-4)(100 x+500)=100 x^2[/math]বা, [math]100 \mathrm{x}^2+500 \mathrm{x}-400 \mathrm{x}-2000=100 \mathrm{x}^2[/math]বা, [math]100 \mathrm{x}=2000[/math] বা, [math]\mathrm{x}=\frac{2000}{100} \therefore \mathrm{x}=20[/math][math]\therefore[/math] সমিতির সদস্য সংখ্যা [math]=20[/math] জনএবং মোট চাঁদার পরিমাণ [math]=100 \mathrm{x}^2[/math] টাকা [math]=100 \times(20)^2[/math] টাকা [math]=100 \times 400[/math] টাকা [math]=40,000[/math] টাকাসদস্য সংখ্যা 20 জন এবং মোট চাঁদার পরিমাণ 40,000 টাকা (Ans.)
গমোট চাঁদার [math]\frac{1}{4}[/math] অংশ [math]=\left(40,000\right.[/math] টাকা এর [math]\left.\frac{1}{4}\right)=10,000[/math] টাকাঅবশিষ্ট টাকার পরিমাণ [math]=(40,000-10,000)[/math] টাকা [math]=30,000[/math] টাকা১ম ক্ষেত্রে মুনাফা [math]=\mathrm{Pnr}=\left(10,000 \times 2 \times \frac{5}{100}\right)[/math] টাকা[ [math]\because \mathrm{P}=10,000[/math] টাকা, [math]\mathrm{n}=2[/math] বছর, [math]\mathrm{r}=5 \%=\frac{5}{100}[/math] টাকা] [math]=1000[/math] টাকা২য় ক্ষেত্রে মুনাফা [math]=\mathrm{Pnr}=\left(30,000 \times 2 \times \frac{4}{100}\right)[/math] টাকা[math]\left[\because \mathrm{P}=30,000\right.[/math] টাকা, [math]\mathrm{n}=2[/math] বছর, [math]\mathrm{r}=4 \%=\frac{4}{100}[/math] টাকা [math]][/math] [math]=2400[/math] টাকা[math]\therefore[/math] মোট মুনাফা [math]=(1000+2400)[/math] টাকা [math]=3400[/math] টাকা (Ans.)
ঘ

Question #25 (ID: 805281)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
বনভোজনে যাওয়ার জন্য একটি বাস 2400 টাকায় ভাড়া করা হলো এবং শর্ত হলো প্রত্যেক যাত্রী সমান ভাড়া বহন করবে। 10 জন যাত্রী না আসায় মাথাপিছু ভাড়া 8 (আট) টাকা বৃদ্ধি পেল।

Options:
ক. মাথাপিছু বর্ধিত ভাড়ার পরিমাণ, না আসা যাত্রী সংখ্যার শতকরা কত তা নির্ণয় কর।
খ. বাসে যাওয়া যাত্রীর মাথাপিছু ভাড়া নির্ণয় কর।
গ. বাস ভাড়ার সমপরিমাণ টাকার 5% হার মুনাফায় 13 বছরের সরল মুনাফা ও চক্রবৃদ্ধি মুনাফার পার্থক্য নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবর্ধিত ভাড়া 8 টাকানা আসা যাত্রী সংখ্যা 10 জন[math]\therefore[/math] বর্ধিত ভাড়া, না আসা যাত্রী সংখ্যার শতকরা [math]=\frac{8}{10} \times 100=80[/math] (Ans.)
খধরি, বাসের যাত্রী সংখ্যা [math]= x[/math][math]\therefore[/math] জন প্রতি ভাড়া [math]=\frac{2400}{\mathrm{x}}[/math] টাকাসব যাত্রী উপস্থিত থাকলে যাত্রী সংখ্যা হত [math](x+10)[/math] জনতখন জনপ্রতি ভাড়া হত [math]\frac{2400}{x+10}[/math] টাকাপ্রশ্নমতে, [math]\frac{2400}{x}-\frac{2400}{x+10}=8[/math] বা, [math]\frac{2400(x+10)-2400 x}{x(x+10)}=8[/math]বা, [math]8 x(x+10)=2400(x+10)-2400 x[/math]বা, [math]8 x(x+10)=2400(x+10-x)[/math]বা, [math]8 \mathrm{x}(\mathrm{x}+10)=2400 \times 10[/math]বা, [math]8 \mathrm{x}(\mathrm{x}+10)=24000[/math] বা,[math]8\left(\mathrm{x}^2+10 \mathrm{x}\right)-24000=0[/math]বা, [math]8\left(x^2+10 x-3000\right)=0[/math]বা, [math]x^2+10 x-3000=0[/math] [উভয়পক্ষকে 8 দ্বারা ভাগ করে]বা, [math]x^2+60 x-50 x-3000=0[/math]বা, [math]x(x+60)-50(x+60)=0[/math]বা, [math](x+60)(x-50)=0[/math]হয়, [math]x+60=0[/math]  অথবা, [math]\mathrm{x}-50=0[/math]অর্থাৎ, [math]x=-60[/math]    [math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{x}=50[/math]যেহেতু [math]x[/math] যাত্রী সংখ্যা নির্দেশ করে। অতএব, তা কখনোই ঋণাত্মক হতে পারে না।[math]\therefore[/math][math]x = 50[/math]অর্থাৎ, বাসে [math]50[/math] জন যাত্রী গিয়েছিল।জন প্রতি ভাড়া[math]=\frac{2400}{50}[/math]টাকা [math]= 48[/math] টাকা[math]\therefore[/math]মাথাপিছু ভাড়া [math]48[/math] টাকা (Ans.)
গদেওয়া আছে, মুনাফার হার, [math]\mathrm{r}=5 \%=\frac{5}{100}=0.05[/math]বাস ভাড়ার সমপরিমাণ টাকা হলো আসল।[math]\therefore[/math] আসল, [math]\mathrm{P}=2400[/math] টাকাসময়, [math]\mathrm{n}=13[/math] বছরআমরা জানি,সরল মুনাফা, [math]\mathrm{I}=\mathrm{Pnr}=(2400 \times 13 \times 0.05)[/math] টাকা [math]=1560[/math] টাকাআবার, চক্রবৃদ্ধি মুনাফা [math]=\mathrm{P}(1+\mathrm{r})^{\mathrm{n}}-\mathrm{P}[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =2400(1+0.05)^{13}-2400\\&amp;=2400(1.05)^{13}-2400 \\&amp; =4525.56-2400=2125.56 \text { টাকা (প্রায়) }\end{aligned}[/math]\therefore[/math] চক্রবৃদ্ধি মুনাফা ও সরল মুনাফার পার্থক্য,[math](2125.56-1560)[/math] টাকা [math]= 565.56[/math] টাকা (প্রায়) (Ans.)
ঘ

Question #26 (ID: 805282)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোনো সংখ্যা ও ঐ সংখ্যার গুণাত্মক বিপরীত সংখ্যার সমষ্টি 3.

Options:
ক. সংখ্যাটিকে x চলকে প্রকাশ করে উপরের তথ্যকে সমীকরণের মাধ্যমে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. [math]x^3-\frac{1}{x^3}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}=123[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কমনে করি, সংখ্যাটি [math]\mathrm x[/math][math]\therefore \mathrm{x}[/math]-এর গুণাত্মক বিপরীত সংখ্যা [math]\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}[/math]প্রশ্নমতে, [math]x+\frac{1}{x}=3[/math] (Ans.)
খ'ক' হতে পাই, [math]\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}=3[/math]এখন, [math]\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2-4 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=(3)^2-4[/math] [মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \therefore\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=5 \therefore x-\frac{1}{x}=\sqrt{5} \\&amp; \text { আবার, } x^3-\frac{1}{x^3}\\&amp;=\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^3+3 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right) \\&amp; \therefore(\sqrt{5})+3 \cdot \sqrt{5}=5 \sqrt{5}+3 \sqrt{5}=8 \sqrt{5} \\&amp; \therefore x^3-\frac{1}{x^3}=8 \sqrt{5} \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
গ'ক' ও 'খ' হতে পাই, [math]\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}=3[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{x}-\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}=\sqrt{5}[/math]এখন [math]\mathrm{x}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^3}=\left(\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\right)^3-3 \cdot \mathrm{x} \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\left(\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\right)[/math][math]\begin{aligned}&amp; =(3)^3-3.3 \text { [মান বসিয়ে] } \\&amp; =27-9=18 \\\therefore x^3+\frac{1}{x^3}=18 &amp; \cdots \cdots \cdots(\mathrm{i})\end{aligned}[/math]এবং [math]x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}=\left(x-\frac{1}{x}\right)^2+2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}=(\sqrt{5})^2+2[/math] [মান বসিয়ে]       [math]=5+2=7[/math][math]\therefore \mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}=7......................[/math](ii)(i) ও (ii) নং সমীকরণ গুণ করে, [math]\left(\mathrm{x}^3+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^3}\right)\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^2}\right)=18 \times 7[/math]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{x^3}{x^2}+\frac{x^2}{x^3}+\frac{1}{x^5}=126[/math] বা, [math]x^5+x+\frac{1}{x}+\frac{1}{x^5}=126[/math]বা, [math]\left(\mathrm{x}^5+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^5}\right)+\left(\mathrm{x}+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}}\right)=126[/math] বা, [math]\mathrm{x}^5+\frac{1}{\mathrm{x}^5}+3=126[/math] [মান বসিয়ে]বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}=126-3[/math] বা, [math]x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}=123 \therefore x^5+\frac{1}{x^5}=123[/math] (প্রমাণিত)

Question #27 (ID: 805283)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(ⅰ) যেকোনো একটি সংখ্যা [math]a[/math] কে বর্গ করে যে মান পাওয়া যায় তার সাথে [math]1[/math] যোগ করলে সংখ্যাটি হয় [math]\sqrt{5} \mathrm{a}[/math].

(ii) [math]\mathrm{x}=38+17 \sqrt{5}[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math](u+v)^3=u^3+v^3+3 u v(u+v)[/math]
খ. [math]\sqrt[3]{x}-\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{x}}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. দেখাও যে, [math]a^7+\frac{1}{a^7}=13 \sqrt{5}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক[math] \text { বামপক্ষ } =(u+v)^3=(u+v)(u+v)^2 \\ =(u+v)\left(u^2+2 u v+v^2\right) \\ =u\left(u^2+2 u v+v^2\right)+v\left(u^2+2 u v+v^2\right) \\ =u^3+2 u^2 v+u v^2+u^2 v+2 u v^2+v^3 \\ =u^3+3 u^2 v+3 u v^2+v^3 \\ =u^3+v^3+3 u v(u+v)=\text { ডানপক্ষ } \\ \therefore(u+v)^3 =u^3+v^3+3 u v(u+v) \text { (প্রমাণিত) }[/math]
খউদ্দীপকের (ii) নং তথ্যানুসারে, [math]x=38+17 \sqrt{5}[/math]বা, [math]x=8+12 \sqrt{5}+30+5 \sqrt{5}[/math]বা, [math]x=2^3+3 \cdot 2^2 \cdot \sqrt{5}+3 \cdot 2 \cdot(\sqrt{5})^2+(\sqrt{5})^3[/math]বা, [math]x=(2+\sqrt{5})^3 \therefore \sqrt[3]{x}=\sqrt{5}+2[/math][math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \therefore \frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{x}}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{5}+2}=\frac{\sqrt{5}-2}{(\sqrt{5}+2)(\sqrt{5}-2)} \\&amp; \quad=\frac{\sqrt{5}-2}{(\sqrt{5})^2-2^2}=\frac{\sqrt{5}-2}{5-4}=\sqrt{5}-2 \\&amp; \therefore \sqrt[3]{x}-\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{x}}=\sqrt{5}+2-\sqrt{5}+2=4 \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
গউদ্দীকের (i) নং তথ্যানুসারে, [math]\mathrm{a}^2+1=\sqrt{5} \mathrm{a}[/math]বা, [math]\frac{a^2}{a}+\frac{1}{a}=\frac{\sqrt{5} a}{a} \therefore a+\frac{1}{a}=\sqrt{5}[/math]এখন, [math]\mathrm{a}^4+\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^4}=\left(\mathrm{a}^2\right)^2+\left(\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^2}\right)^2\\=\left(\mathrm{a}^2+\frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^2}\right)^2-2 \cdot \mathrm{a}^2 \cdot \frac{1}{\mathrm{a}^2}[math]=\left\{\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^2-2 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}\right\}^2-2\\=\left\{(\sqrt{5})^2-2\right\}^2-2[/math]=(5-2)^2-2=9-2=7[/math][math]\therefore a^4+\frac{1}{a^4}=7...........[/math](i)[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \therefore a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}=\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right)^3-3 \cdot a \cdot \frac{1}{a}\left(a+\frac{1}{a}\right) \\&amp; =(\sqrt{5})^3-3 \sqrt{5}=5 \sqrt{5}-3 \sqrt{5} \\&amp; \therefore a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}=2 \sqrt{5} \ldots \ldots \text { (ii) }\end{aligned}[/math]সমীকরণ (i) ও (ii) গুণ করে পাই,[math]\left(a^4+\frac{1}{a^4}\right)\left(a^3+\frac{1}{a^3}\right)=7 \times 2 \sqrt{5}\\ \text { বা, } a^7+a+\frac{1}{a}+\frac{1}{a^7}=14 \sqrt{5}[/math]বা, [math]a^7+\frac{1}{a^7}=14 \sqrt{5}-\sqrt{5} \therefore a^7+\frac{1}{a^7}=13 \sqrt{5}[/math]
ঘ

Question #28 (ID: 805284)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: গণিত | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm A=x+y+z, \mathrm B=x y+2 x z+2 y z,[/math][math]\mathrm P=x^4+x^2 y^2+y^4[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{Q}=\mathrm{x}^2-\mathrm{xy}+\mathrm{y}^2[/math]

Options:
ক. সরল কর:[math]<br />
(m+n-p)^2+(m-n+p)^2[/math][math]-2(m-n+p)(m+n-p)<br />
[/math]
খ. [math]\mathrm{A}=6-\mathrm{z}, \mathrm{B}=3[/math] হলে, [math]\mathrm{x}^2+\mathrm{y}^2+4 \mathrm{z}^2[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\mathrm{P}=35[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{Q}=7[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y}= \pm 2 \sqrt{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি: [math](m+n-p)^2+(m-n+p)^2\\-2(m-n+p)(m+n-p)[/math][math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \text { [ধরি, } x=m+n-p, y=m-n+p] \\&amp; =x^2+y^2-2 y \cdot x=(x-y)^2\\&amp;=\{m+n-p-(m-n+p)\}^2 \\&amp; =(m+n-p-m+n-p)^2 \\&amp; =(2 n-2 p)^2=4 n^2-8 n p+4 p^2 \text { (Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{A}=\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y}+\mathrm{z}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{B}=\mathrm{xy}+2 \mathrm{xz}+2 \mathrm{yz}[/math][math]\therefore \quad x+y+z=6-z \cdots \cdots \cdots \text { (i) }[/math]এবং [math]x y+2 x z+2 y z=3.............[/math](ii)(i) নং থেকে, [math]x+y+2 z=6[/math]বা, [math]x^2+y^2+4 z^2+2 x y+4 y z+4 x z=36[/math] [বর্গ করে]বা, [math]x^2+y^2+4 z^2+2(x y+2 y z+2 x z)=36[/math]বা, [math]x^2+y^2+4 z^2+2.3=36[/math] [(i) নং হতে মান বসিয়ে]বা, [math]x^2+y^2+4 z^2=36-6 \therefore x^2+y^2+4 z^2=30[/math] (Ans.)
গপ্রশ্নমতে, [math]\mathrm{Q}=\mathrm{x}^2-\mathrm{xy}+\mathrm{y}^2=7...........[/math](iii)এবং [math]\mathrm{P}=35[/math] বা, [math]\mathrm{x}^4+\mathrm{x}^2 \mathrm{y}^2+\mathrm{y}^4=35[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^2\right)^2+2 x^2 y^2+\left(y^2\right)^2-x^2 y^2=35[/math]বা, [math]\left(x^2+y^2\right)^2-(x y)^2=35[/math] বা, [math]\left(x^2+y^2+x y\right)\left(x^2+y^2-x y\right)=35[/math]বা, [math]7\left(\mathrm{x}^2+\mathrm{y}^2+\mathrm{xy}\right)=35[/math] [(iii) নং হতে মান বসিয়ে][math]\therefore x^2+x y+y^2=5........[/math](iv)(iii) নং থেকে (iv) নং বিয়োগ করে পাই,[math]x^2-x y+y^2-x^2-y^2-x y=7-5[/math]বা, [math]-2 x y=2 \therefore x y=-1[/math](iii) ও (iv) নং যোগ করে পাই, [math]2 x^2+2 y^2=7+5[/math]বা, [math]x^2+y^2=6[/math] বা, [math](x-y)^2+2 x y=6[/math]বা, [math](x-y)^2+2(-1)=6[/math] বা, [math](x-y)^2=6+2=8[/math]বা, [math]x-y= \pm \sqrt{8}= \pm \sqrt{4 \times 2} \therefore x-y= \pm 2 \sqrt{2}[/math] (দেখানো হলো)

Question #29 (ID: 805285)

Question:
[math]a+\frac{1}{a+2}=3, x^3+y^3=m[/math] এবং [math]x^2+y^2=n[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]x-y=\mathrm P[/math] হলে [math]x y[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রমাণ কর যে，[math](\mathrm{a}+2)^5+\frac{1}{(\mathrm{a}+2)^5}=2525.[/math]
গ. [math]m=8[/math] এবং [math]n=4[/math] হলে，[math](x+y)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]x^2+y^2=n \ldots . . . . .[/math](i)[math]x-y=\sqrt{P}[/math] হলে, [math]x^2+y^2-2 x y=P[/math]বা, [math]n-2 x y=P[/math] বা, [math]2 x y=n-p[/math] বা, [math]x y=\frac{n-p}{2}[/math]
খদেওয়া আছে, [math]a+\frac{1}{a+2}=3[/math] বা, [math](a+2)+\frac{1}{(a+2)}=3+2[/math]বা, [math](a+2)+\frac{1}{(a+2)}=5[/math] [math].......[/math](i)বা, [math]\left\{(a+2)+\frac{1}{(a+2)}\right\}^2=5^2[/math]বা, [math](a+2)^2+\frac{1}{(a+2)^2}+2 \cdot(a+2) \cdot \frac{1}{(a+2)}=25[math]\therefore (a+2)^2+\frac{1}{(a+2)^2}=25-2=23.........[/math](ii)আবার, [math](\mathrm{a}+2)^3+\frac{1}{(\mathrm{a}+2)^3}=\left\{(\mathrm{a}+2)+\frac{1}{(\mathrm{a}+2)}\right\}^3[/math]\begin{aligned}-3 \cdot(\mathrm{a}+2) \cdot \frac{1}{(\mathrm{a}+2)}\{ &amp; \left.(\mathrm{a}+2)+\frac{1}{(\mathrm{a}+2)}\right\} \\&amp; =(5)^3-3.5 \text { [(i) হতে] } \\&amp; =125-15\end{aligned}[/math][math]\therefore \quad(a+3)^3+\frac{1}{(a+2)^3}=110..........[/math](iii)(ii) ও (iii) গুণ করে পাই,[math]\begin{aligned}&amp; \left\{(a+2)^2+\frac{1}{(a+2)^2}\right\}\left\{(a+2)^3+\frac{1}{(a+2)^3}\right\}\\&amp;=23 \times 110 \\&amp; \text { বা, } (a+2)^5+\frac{1}{(a+2)^5}+\frac{1}{(a+2)}+(a+2)\\&amp;=2530 \\&amp; \text { বা, } (a+2)^5+\frac{1}{(a+2)^5}+5=2530 \\&amp; \therefore (a+2)^5+\frac{1}{(a+2)^5}=2525 \text { (প্রমাণিত) }\end{aligned}[/math]
গপ্রশ্নমতে, [math]x^3+y^3=8...........[/math](i)      [math]x^2+y^2=4..........[/math](ii)(i) করে পাই, [math](x+y)^3-3 x y(x+y)=8[/math] [math].......[/math](iii)(ii) হতে পাই, [math](x+y)^2-2 x y=4[/math]বা, [math]2 x y=(x+y)^2-4[/math] বা, [math]x y=\frac{1}{2}\left\{(x+y)^2-4\right\}[/math](iii) নং সমীকরণে [math]x y[/math] এর মান বসিয়ে,[math](x+y)^3-3 \times \frac{1}{2}\left\{(x+y)^2-4\right\}(x+y)=8[/math]বা, [math]a^3-\frac{3}{2}\left(a^2-4\right) \cdot a=8[x+y=a[/math] ধরে[math]][/math]বা, [math]2 a^3-3\left(a^2-4\right) \cdot a=16[/math] বা, [math]2 a^3-3 a^3+12 a=16[/math]বা, [math]-a^3+12 a=16[/math] বা, [math]a^3-12 a+16=0[/math]বা, [math]a^3-2 a^2+2 a^2-4 a-8 a+16=0[/math]বা, [math]a^2(a-2)+2 a(a-2)-8(a-2)=0[/math]বা, [math](a-2)\left(a^2+2 a-8\right)=0[/math] বা, [math](a-2)\left(a^2+4 a-2 a-8\right)=0[/math]বা, [math](\mathrm{a}-2)\{\mathrm{a}(\mathrm{a}+4)-2(\mathrm{a}+4)\}=0[/math]বা, [math](a-2)(a+4)(a-2)=0[/math] বা, [math](a-2)^2(a+4)=0[/math]হয়, [math](a - 2) ^ 2 = 0[/math]     অথবা [math](a + 4) = 0[/math]বা, [math]a - 2 = 0[/math]           বা, [math]a = - 4[/math]বা, [math]a = 2[/math]             [math]\therefore[/math][math]x + y = - 4[math]\therefore[/math][math]x + y = 2[/math]\therefore[/math] [math](x + y)[/math] এর মান [math]2[/math] অথবা [math]&ndash; 4[/math] (Ans.)
